		function getKeyStatus()
			secretNames = {"premium","Premium","og boi"};
			if (table.find(premOG(script_key .. "-tetrax"), lpuserid) or (keyNote[1] == secretNames[v084("table.find")(secretNames, keyNote[1])])) then
				return "premium";
			else
				return "regular";
			end
		end
		function getTitleNamePart()
			secretNames = {"premium","Premium","og boi"};
			if (getKeyStatus() == "premium") then
				return "\240\159\145\145\10";
			elseif (keyNote[1] == "Ad Reward") then
				return "FREE";
			elseif ((keyNote[1] == "regular") or (keyNote[1] == "Regular")) then
				return "";
			end
		end
		function GetWindowIcon()
			local v0 = nil;
			local Icon = nil;
			for l, v in next, {"Premium","premium","premium ","Premium "} do
				if (keyNote[1] == v) then
					v0 = true;
					Icon = "crown";
					break;
				end
			end
			if ((v0 == nil) and table.find(premOG(script_key .. "-tetrax"), lpuserid)) then
				v0 = true;
				Icon = "crown";
			end
			if ((v0 == nil) and (keyNote[1] == "Ad Reward")) then
				v0 = true;
				Icon = nil;
			end
			return Icon, v0;
		end
		function GetMode(value, bool)
			if (value == "selectedplrsmode") then
				if (bool == "auto teleport") then
					return "teleporting";
				elseif (bool == "kill") then
					return "killing";
				elseif (bool == "spectate") then
					return "spectating";
				elseif (bool == "loopbring") then
					return "bringing";
				elseif (bool == "gun kill") then
					return "gun killing";
				elseif (bool == "blade kill") then
					return 'blade kill'
				else
					return "N/A";
				end
			end
		end
		function GetFullPlayerString(p, y)
			if (y == nil) and z001 and z001.players and z001.players.playersinfo then
				if (GetMode("selectedplrsmode", p) == "killing") then
					if (selectedplr ~= nil) then
						local trsn = tcmod == nil and "name: " .. selectedplr .. '\n' .. 'cash: ' .. ('$'..getPlayerCash(selectedplr) or '$ 0')  .. '\n' .. "mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode) .. "\n" .. "attack position: " .. selectedplrpos or
						tcmod == 'chinese' and "名字: " .. selectedplr .. '\n' .. '资产: ' .. ('$'..getPlayerCash(selectedplr) or '$ 0')  .. '\n' .. "模式: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode) .. "\n" .. "attack position: " .. selectedplrpos
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetTitle("player selected");
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc(trsn);
					else
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc("mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode) .. "\n" .. "attack position: " .. selectedplrpos);
					end
				elseif (GetMode("selectedplrsmode", p) == "teleporting") then
					if (selectedplr ~= nil) then
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetTitle("player selected");
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc("name: " .. selectedplr .. '\n' .. 'cash: ' .. ('$'..getPlayerCash(selectedplr) or '$ 0')  .. '\n' .. "mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode) .. "\n" .. "position: " .. selectedplrpos);
					else
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc("mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode) .. "\n" .. "position: " .. selectedplrpos);
					end
				elseif (GetMode("selectedplrsmode", p) == "spectating") then
					if (selectedplr ~= nil) then
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetTitle("player selected");
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc("name: " .. selectedplr .. '\n' .. 'cash: ' .. ('$'..getPlayerCash(selectedplr) or '$ 0')  .. "\n" .. "mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode));
					else
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc("mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode));
					end
				elseif (GetMode("selectedplrsmode", p) == "bringing") then
					if (selectedplr ~= nil) then
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetTitle("player selected");
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc("name: " .. selectedplr .. '\n' .. 'cash: ' .. ('$'..getPlayerCash(selectedplr) or '$ 0')  .. "\n" .. "mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode));
					else
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc("mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode));
					end
				elseif (GetMode("selectedplrsmode", p) == "gun killing") then
					if (selectedplr ~= nil) then
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetTitle("player selected");
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc("name: " .. selectedplr .. '\n' .. 'cash: ' .. ('$'..getPlayerCash(selectedplr) or '$ 0') .. "\n" .. "mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode));
					else
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc("mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode));
					end
				elseif (GetMode("selectedplrsmode", p) == "blade kill") then
					if (selectedplr ~= nil) then
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetTitle("player selected");
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc("name: " .. selectedplr .. '\n' .. 'cash: ' .. ('$'..getPlayerCash(selectedplr) or '$ 0') .. "\n" .. "mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode));
					else
						z001.players.playersinfo:SetDesc("mode: " .. GetMode("selectedplrsmode", selectedplrsmode));
					end
				end
			end
		end
		function GetByDisplayName(name)
			if (name ~= nil) then
				for l, v in next, players:GetPlayers() do
					if (name == v.DisplayName) then
						return v.Name;
					end
				end
			end
		end
		function GetPlayersNames()
			local plrscache = {};
			for l, v in next, service.Players:GetPlayers() do
				if (v.Name ~= lpname) then
					table.insert(plrscache, v.Name);
				end
			end
			table.sort(plrscache)
			return plrscache;
		end
		function ShowChatLogs(value)
			if TextChatService.ChatWindowConfiguration then
				TextChatService.ChatWindowConfiguration.Enabled = value;
			end
		end
		function GetAvailablePositions(value, funcpos, x, y, z)
			local k = {unhidden=function()
				return CFrame.new(0, 20, 0);
			end,hidden=function()
				return CFrame.new(0, -20, 0);
			end,custom=function(mover1, mover2, mover3)
				local mov1 = mover1 or 0;
				local mov2 = mover2 or 0;
				local mov3 = mover3 or 0;
				return CFrame.new(mov1, mov2, mov3);
			end};
			if (value == nil) then
				local o = {};
				for l, v in next, k do
					table.insert(o, l);
				end
				return o;
			elseif ((value == true) and (funcpos ~= nil) and (k[funcpos] ~= nil)) then
				return k[funcpos];
			end
		end
		function checkforerror(r,g,erro,info)
			if r == false and info and info.currentline then
				return g(erro,'\n error line: ' ..info.currentline)
			elseif r == false and not info then
				return g(erro)
			end
		end		
		function GetAvailablePlrsModes()
			local vm={"kill","spectate","auto teleport","loopbring","gun kill","blade kill"}
			table.sort(vm)
			return vm;
		end

		function FlyButton()
			if ((UserInputService.TouchEnabled and not UserInputService.KeyboardEnabled and not UserInputService.MouseEnabled) or (string.find(v084('identifyexecutor')(), "Delta") and UserInputService.KeyboardEnabled and UserInputService.MouseEnabled)) then
				if not CoreGui:FindFirstChild("TeTraX-Fly") then
					local ScreenGui1 = Instance.new("ScreenGui");
					ScreenGui1.Name = "TeTraX-Fly";
					ScreenGui1.Parent = CoreGui;
					ScreenGui1.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling;
					local ImageButton1 = Instance.new("TextButton");
					ImageButton1.Text = "X-Fly";
					ImageButton1.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(44, 44, 44);
					ImageButton1.BorderSizePixel = 3;
					ImageButton1.Parent = ScreenGui1;
					ImageButton1.Transparency = 0.9;
					ImageButton1.Position = UDim2.new(0.08, 0, 0.5, 0);
					ImageButton1.Size = UDim2.new(0, 63, 0, 63);
					ImageButton1.TextSize = 25;
					ImageButton1.FontFace = Font.new([[rbxasset://fonts/families/Bangers.json]], Enum.FontWeight.Regular, Enum.FontStyle.Normal);
					ImageButton1.Draggable = true;
					loadU:CreateConnection("FlyButtonDown", ImageButton1.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
						isFlyActive = not isFlyActive;
						FlyInstances();
					end));
					local UICornersc = Instance.new("UICorner", ImageButton1);
					UICornersc.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0, 1, 0);
					local UIGradiennt = Instance.new("UIGradient", ImageButton1);
					UIGradiennt.Color = selectedcolor();
					local windowuistrokes = Instance.new("UIStroke", ImageButton1);
					windowuistrokes.Name = "FlyStroke";
					windowuistrokes.Thickness = 1;
					windowuistrokes.ApplyStrokeMode = "Contextual";
					windowuistrokes.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1);
					windowuistrokes.Transparency = 0;
					local ww = Instance.new("UIGradient", windowuistrokes);
					ww.Name = "FlyGrad";
					ww.Color = selectedcolor();
					local windowuistroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", ImageButton1);
					windowuistroke.Thickness = 2.5;
					windowuistroke.ApplyStrokeMode = "Border";
					windowuistroke.Color = Color3.new(1, 1, 1);
					windowuistroke.Transparency = 0;
					local UIGradientsc = Instance.new("UIGradient", windowuistroke);
					UIGradientsc.Color = selectedcolor();
					local GlowRadiant = Instance.new("UIGradient", windowuistroke);
					GlowRadiant.Color = selectedcolor();
					local i0 =  ImageButton1:FindFirstChild("UIStroke")
					local i1 = i0:FindFirstChild("UIGradient")
					local i2 = ImageButton1:FindFirstChild("FlyStroke")
					local i3 = i2:FindFirstChild("FlyGrad")

					loadU:CreateConnection("FlyButtonStepped", RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(deltaTime)
						local result, _ = pcall(function()
							if (ImageButton1 and i0 and i1 and i2 and i3) then
								local uiGradient = ImageButton1.UIStroke.UIGradient;
								uiGradient.Rotation = (uiGradient.Rotation + 1) % 360;
								uiGradient.Color = selectedcolor();
								local uitxtgea = ImageButton1.FlyStroke.FlyGrad;
								uitxtgea.Color = selectedcolor();
								uitxtgea.Rotation = (uitxtgea.Rotation + 1) % 360;
							end
						end);
						if (result == false) then
							checkforerror(result,v084('warn'), _,v084('getinfo')(2,'nl'));
							loadU:CleanConnection("FlyButtonStepped");
							result = nil;
						end
					end)));
				end
			end
		end




		-- [[ GET REMOTE SIGNALS ]] -- 
		function getremoteinstance(d)
			local load = getLoader('Signal')
			if load.InvokeServer ~= nil then
				local upvalues = v084('getupvalues')(load.LinkSignal)[1]
				for l,v in next,upvalues do
					if l == d then
						return v 
					end
				end
			end
		end

		GetMoveVector = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			if (controlModule and (controlModule.GetMoveVector ~= nil)) then
				return controlModule:GetMoveVector();
			end
		end)
		function FireServer(event, ...)
			-- local args = {...}
			-- if (args and (typeof(...) == "table")) then
			-- 	getLoader('Signal').FireServer(event, unpack(...));
			-- else
				getLoader('Signal').FireServer(event, ...);
		end
		function InvokeServer(event, args)
			if (args and (typeof(args) == "table")) then
				return getLoader('Signal').InvokeServer(event, unpack(args));
			else
				return getLoader('Signal').InvokeServer(event, args);
			end
		end
		function ClientReplicator(kind, val1, val2, value)
			if ((kind == "Set") and (value ~= nil)) then
				return getLoader("ClientReplicator")[kind](val1, val2, value);
			elseif ((kind == "Get") and (val2 ~= nil)) then
				return getLoader("ClientReplicator")[kind] and getLoader("ClientReplicator")[kind](val1, val2);
			elseif ((kind == "Replicate") and (val1 ~= nil)) then
				return getLoader("ClientReplicator")[kind](val1);
			end
		end
		function ItemCheck()
			local j = {};
			local inv = getLoader("v3item").inventory and getLoader("v3item").inventory.currentItemsData;
			for l, v in next, inv or {} do
				if not v.isStashed then
					table.insert(j, v.name);
				end
			end
			return j;
		end
		function addnumbers(num1,num2)
			return num1 + num2
		end
		refreshAllPlayerData = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			local newData = {totalMoneyPrinters=0,totalLegendarieSkins=0,totalMythicSkins=0,totalEpicSkins=0,totalRareSkins=0,totalCommonSkins=0,totalSkins=0,totalAmountLegendary=0,totalAmountMythic=0,totalAmountEpic=0,totalAmountRare=0,totalAmountCommon=0,totalAmount=0,totalRareGems=0,totalAmountRareGems=0,totalDiamonds=0,totalDiamondOre=0,totalRollies=0,totalDiamondRings=0,totalDarkMatterGems=0,totalVoidGems=0,totalGoldCrowns=0,totalGoldCups=0,totalAmountDiamonds=0,totalAmountDiamondOre=0,totalAmountRollies=0,totalAmountDiamondRings=0,totalAmountDarkMatterGems=0,totalAmountVoidGems=0,totalAmountGoldCrowns=0,totalAmountGoldCups=0};
			for o, p in next, refreshSkins() do
				for k, v in next, p do
					if (checkRarity(k) == "Legendary") then
						newData.totalLegendarieSkins = newData.totalLegendarieSkins + v;
						newData.totalAmountLegendary = newData.totalAmountLegendary + getSkinPrices(k);
					elseif (checkRarity(k) == "Epic") then
						newData.totalEpicSkins = newData.totalEpicSkins + v;
						newData.totalAmountEpic = newData.totalAmountEpic + getSkinPrices(k);
					elseif (checkRarity(k) == "Mythic") then
						newData.totalMythicSkins = newData.totalMythicSkins + v;
						newData.totalAmountMythic = newData.totalAmountMythic + getSkinPrices(k);
					elseif (checkRarity(k) == "Rare") then
						newData.totalRareSkins = newData.totalRareSkins + v;
						newData.totalAmountRare = newData.totalAmountRare + getSkinPrices(k);
					elseif (checkRarity(k) == "Common") then
						newData.totalCommonSkins = newData.totalCommonSkins + v;
						newData.totalAmountCommon = newData.totalAmountCommon + getSkinPrices(k);
					end
					newData.totalSkins = newData.totalSkins + v;
					newData.totalAmount = newData.totalAmount + getSkinPrices(k);
				end
			end
			if (getLoader("v3item") and getLoader("v3item").inventory and getLoader("v3item").inventory.items) then
				for _, v in next, getLoader("v3item").inventory.items do
					if (v and (v.name == "Money Printer")) then
						newData.totalMoneyPrinters = newData.totalMoneyPrinters + v.ammoManager.ammo;
					elseif (v and (v.name == "Gold Cup")) then
						newData.totalGoldCups = newData.totalGoldCups + v.ammoManager.ammo;
						newData.totalAmountGoldCups = newData.totalAmountGoldCups + (getGemPrice(v.name) * v.ammoManager.ammo or 0);
					elseif (v and (v.name == "Gold Crown")) then
						newData.totalGoldCrowns = newData.totalGoldCrowns + v.ammoManager.ammo;
						newData.totalAmountGoldCrowns = newData.totalAmountGoldCrowns + (getGemPrice(v.name) * v.ammoManager.ammo or 0);
					elseif (v and (v.name == "Diamond")) then
						newData.totalDiamonds = newData.totalDiamonds + v.ammoManager.ammo;
						newData.totalAmountDiamonds = newData.totalAmountDiamonds + (getGemPrice(v.name) * v.ammoManager.ammo or 0);
					elseif (v and (v.name == "Diamond Ore")) then
						newData.totalDiamondOre = newData.totalDiamondOre + v.ammoManager.ammo;
						newData.totalAmountDiamondOre = newData.totalAmountDiamondOre + (getGemPrice(v.name) * v.ammoManager.ammo or 0);
					elseif (v and (v.name == "Dark Matter Gem")) then
						newData.totalDarkMatterGems = newData.totalDarkMatterGems + v.ammoManager.ammo;
						newData.totalAmountDarkMatterGems = newData.totalAmountDarkMatterGems + (getGemPrice(v.name) * v.ammoManager.ammo or 0);
					elseif (v and (v.name == "Void Gem")) then
						newData.totalVoidGems = newData.totalVoidGems + v.ammoManager.ammo;
						newData.totalAmountVoidGems = newData.totalAmountVoidGems + (getGemPrice(v.name) * v.ammoManager.ammo or 0);
					elseif (v and (v.name == "Rollie")) then
						newData.totalRollies = newData.totalRollies + v.ammoManager.ammo;
						newData.totalAmountRollies = newData.totalAmountRollies + (getGemPrice(v.name) * v.ammoManager.ammo or 0);
					end
					if (getRareGems()[v.name] ~= nil) then
						newData.totalRareGems = newData.totalRareGems + v.ammoManager.ammo ;
						newData.totalAmountRareGems = newData.totalAmountRareGems + (getGemPrice(v.name) * v.ammoManager.ammo or 0);
					end
				end
				local currentHouse = getHouse(true)
				local clienthouse = getLoader('clienthouse')
				local v17 = workspace and workspace:FindFirstChild('HousingPlots')
				if currentHouse and v17 ~= nil then
					local e7 = clienthouse.houseData and clienthouse.houseData.house ~= nil and clienthouse.houseData.house.modelName or "DefaultHouse"
					local str = v17:FindFirstChild(currentHouse.Name) and v17[currentHouse.Name]:GetAttribute('owner') == lpuserid and v17[currentHouse.Name]:FindFirstChild('Building') and v17[currentHouse.Name].Building:FindFirstChild(e7) 
					if str and str:FindFirstChild('Furniture') then
						for l,v in next,str.Furniture:GetChildren() do
							for k,m in next,v:GetChildren() do
								if string.find(m.Name, "GemPlacement") then
									local gemName = m:GetAttribute('gemName')
									if gemName == 'Rollie' then
										newData.totalRollies = newData.totalRollies + 1
										newData.totalAmountRollies = newData.totalAmountRollies + getGemPrice(gemName)
										newData.totalRareGems = newData.totalRareGems + 1;
										newData.totalAmountRareGems = newData.totalAmountRareGems + (getGemPrice(gemName) or 0);
									elseif gemName == 'Diamond' then
										newData.totalDiamonds = newData.totalDiamonds + 1
										newData.totalAmountDiamonds = newData.totalAmountDiamonds + getGemPrice(gemName)
										newData.totalRareGems = newData.totalRareGems + 1;
										newData.totalAmountRareGems = newData.totalAmountRareGems + (getGemPrice(gemName) or 0);
									elseif gemName == 'Diamond Ring' then
										newData.totalDiamondRings = newData.totalDiamondRings + 1
										newData.totalAmountDiamondRings = newData.totalAmountDiamondRings + getGemPrice(gemName)
										newData.totalRareGems = newData.totalRareGems + 1;
										newData.totalAmountRareGems = newData.totalAmountRareGems + (getGemPrice(gemName) or 0);
									elseif gemName == 'Void Gem' then
										newData.totalVoidGems = newData.totalVoidGems + 1;	
										newData.totalAmountVoidGems = newData.totalAmountVoidGems + getGemPrice(gemName)
										newData.totalRareGems = newData.totalRareGems + 1;
										newData.totalAmountRareGems = newData.totalAmountRareGems + (getGemPrice(gemName) or 0);
									elseif gemName == 'Dark Matter Gem' then
										newData.totalDarkMatterGems = newData.totalDarkMatterGems + 1;
										newData.totalAmountDarkMatterGems = newData.totalAmountDarkMatterGems + getGemPrice(gemName)
										newData.totalRareGems = newData.totalRareGems + 1;
										newData.totalAmountRareGems = newData.totalAmountRareGems + (getGemPrice(gemName) or 0);
									elseif gemName == 'Diamond Ore' then
										newData.totalDiamondOre = newData.totalDiamondOre + 1;
										newData.totalAmountDiamondOre = newData.totalAmountDiamondOre + getGemPrice(gemName)
										newData.totalRareGems = newData.totalRareGems + 1;
										newData.totalAmountRareGems = newData.totalAmountRareGems + (getGemPrice(gemName) or 0);
									elseif gemName == 'Gold Crown' then
										newData.totalGoldCrowns = newData.totalGoldCrowns + 1;
										newData.totalAmountGoldCrowns = newData.totalAmountGoldCrowns + getGemPrice(gemName)
										newData.totalRareGems = newData.totalRareGems + 1;
										newData.totalAmountRareGems = newData.totalAmountRareGems + (getGemPrice(gemName) or 0);
									elseif gemName == 'Gold Cup' then
										newData.totalGoldCups = newData.totalGoldCups + 1;
										newData.totalAmountGoldCups = newData.totalAmountGoldCups + getGemPrice(gemName)
										newData.totalRareGems = newData.totalRareGems + 1;
										newData.totalAmountRareGems = newData.totalAmountRareGems + (getGemPrice(gemName) or 0);
									end
								end
							end
						end
					end
				end
			end
			local state = getLoader("state");
			newData.skinNetworth = getSkinNetworth(newData);
			newData.playerCash = getohiocashvalue() or 0;
			newData.lastbannedby = checkforAnticheatBan() or "none";
			newData.totalbans = (state and state.data and state.data.numshadowbans) or 0;
			newData.totalatmsrobbed = (state and state.data and state.data.atmsRobbed) or 0;
			newData.totalmoneyearn = (getohiocashvalue() or 0) - 100;
			_cachedPlayerData = newData;
			_lastPlayerDataRefreshTime = tick();
		end);
		PlayerData = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(str)
			if ((tick() - _lastPlayerDataRefreshTime) >= PLAYER_DATA_REFRESH_INTERVAL) then
				refreshAllPlayerData();
			end
			local value = _cachedPlayerData[str];
			if (value == nil) then
				return nil;
			end
			if (typeof(getLoader("commavalue")) == "function") then
				if ((str == "totalatmsrobbed") or (str == "skinNetworth") or (str == "playerCash") or (str == "totalAmount") or (str == "totalAmountCommon") or (str == "totalAmountRare") or (str == "totalAmountEpic") or (str == "totalAmountMythic") or (str == "totalAmountLegendary") or (str == "totalSkins") or (str == "totalLegendarieSkins") or (str == "totalMythicSkins") or (str == "totalEpicSkins") or (str == "totalRareSkins") or (str == "totalCommonSkins") or (str == "totalAmountRareGems") or (str == "totalAmountDiamonds") or (str == "totalAmountDiamondOre") or (str == "totalAmountRollies") or (str == "totalAmountDiamondRings") or (str == "totalAmountDarkMatterGems") or (str == "totalAmountVoidGems") or (str == "totalAmountGoldCrowns") or (str == "totalAmountGoldCups") or (str == "totalRareGems") or (str == "totalDiamonds") or (str == "totalDiamondOre") or (str == "totalRollies") or (str == "totalDiamondRings") or (str == "totalDarkMatterGems") or (str == "totalVoidGems") or (str == "totalGoldCrowns") or (str == "totalGoldCups") or (str == "totalMoneyPrinters") or (str == "totalmoneyearn")) then
					return getLoader("commavalue")(value);
				else
					return value;
				end
			else
				return value;
			end
		end);
		refreshSkins = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			if getLoader("state").data then
				return getLoader("state").data.ownedSkins;
			end
			return {};
		end)
		checkRarity = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(rar)
			if (getLoader("skins").skinData[rar] and getLoader("skins").skinData[rar].rarity) then
				return getLoader("skins").skinData[rar].rarity;
			end
			return nil;
		end)
		function getohiocashvalue()
			if lp:FindFirstChild("stats") then
				return lp.stats.Money.Value;
			else
				return nil;
			end
		end
		getSkinPrices = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(v58)
			local v60 = getLoader("skins").skinData[v58];
			local v61 = getLoader("globals").SKIN_SELL_CASH[v60.rarity] or 0;
			if (v60 and v60.sellPriceOverride) then
				v61 = v60.sellPriceOverride;
			end
			if (v60 and v60.sellPriceModifier) then
				v61 = math.floor(v61 * v60.sellPriceModifier);
			end
			return v61;
		end)
		function checkforAnticheatBan()
			if (getLoader("state") ~= nil) then
				local state_data = getLoader("state");
				if (state_data and state_data.data) then
					local numshadowbans_val = state_data.data.numshadowbans;
					local shadowbanned_modId_val = state_data.data.shadowbanned_modId;
					if ((numshadowbans_val ~= nil) and (numshadowbans_val > 0)) then
						if (shadowbanned_modId_val == nil) then
							return "anti-cheat";
						else
							return shadowbanned_modId_val;
						end
					end
				end
			end
			return nil;
		end
		getSkinNetworth = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(num)
			return (num.totalAmountLegendary + num.totalAmountMythic + num.totalAmountEpic + num.totalAmountRare + num.totalAmount) or 0;
		end);
		getRareGems = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			local _cachegems = {};
			for l, v in next, getLoader("v3items").items do
				if (v.data and (v.data.unpurchasable == true) and (v.data.sellPrice ~= nil) and (v.data.sellPrice >= 900) and (v.data.subtype ~= nil) and (_cachegems[table.find(_cachegems, v.data.subtype)] == nil)) then
					if ((v.data.subtype == "valuable") or (v.data.subtype == "gem")) then
						_cachegems[l] = v.data;
					end
				end
			end
			return _cachegems;
		end);
		function getGemPrice(gem)
			if (getRareGems()[gem] ~= nil) then
				return getRareGems()[gem].sellPrice;
			end
			return 0;
		end
		format_full_date = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(dt_obj, use_utc)
			if (not dt_obj or (dt_obj.UnixTimestamp == 0)) then
				return "N/A";
			end
			local target_dt_obj = nil;
			local success_convert, converted_dt = pcall(function()
				if use_utc then
					return dt_obj:ToUniversalTime();
				else
					return dt_obj:ToLocalTime();
				end
			end);
			if (not success_convert or not converted_dt) then
				return "Error converting date";
			end
			target_dt_obj = converted_dt;
			local year, month, day, hour, minute, second;
			year = target_dt_obj.Year;
			month = target_dt_obj.Month;
			day = target_dt_obj.Day;
			hour = target_dt_obj.Hour;
			minute = target_dt_obj.Minute;
			second = target_dt_obj.Second;
			if ((type(year) ~= "number") or (type(month) ~= "number") or (type(day) ~= "number") or (type(hour) ~= "number") or (type(minute) ~= "number") or (type(second) ~= "number")) then
				return "invalid date components";
			end
			local success, formatted_string = pcall(function()
				return string.format("%02d/%02d/%04d %02d:%02d:%02d", month, day, year, hour, minute, second);
			end);
			if not success then
				return "error formatting date";
			end
			return formatted_string;
		end)
		get_remaining_time_seconds = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			local remaining = function()
				return banEND_unix - current_server_time_unix();
			end;
			return math.max(0, remaining());
		end)
		function GetBanTimeRemaining()
			local remaining_seconds = get_remaining_time_seconds();
			if (remaining_seconds > 0) then
				getgenv().isBanActive = true;
				local days = math.floor(remaining_seconds / (60 * 60 * 24));
				local hours = math.floor((remaining_seconds % (60 * 60 * 24)) / (60 * 60));
				local minutes = math.floor((remaining_seconds % (60 * 60)) / 60);
				local seconds = math.floor(remaining_seconds % 60);
				return string.format("%d days,%d hours,%d minutes,%d seconds", days, hours, minutes, seconds);
			else
				getgenv().isBanActive = false;
				return "ban has expired or is not active.";
			end
		end
		getSkinLogString = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(value,timeskin)
			if value == true then
				if ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild('devv') then
					return "cash: $" .. PlayerData("playerCash") .. "\n" .. "atmsrobbed: " .. PlayerData("totalatmsrobbed") .. '\n'..'skin log available: '..timeskin
				else
					return 'unavailable'
				end
			elseif typeof(value) ~='string' and value ~= true and timeskin == nil then
				if ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild('devv') then
					return "cash: $" .. PlayerData("playerCash") .. "\n" .. "atmsrobbed: " .. PlayerData("totalatmsrobbed") .. "\n" .. "legendary: " .. PlayerData("totalLegendarieSkins") .. "\n" .. "mythic: " .. PlayerData("totalMythicSkins") .. "\n" .. "epic: " .. PlayerData("totalEpicSkins") .. "\n" .. "rare: " .. PlayerData("totalRareSkins") .. "\n" .. "common: " .. PlayerData("totalCommonSkins") .. "\n" .. "total: " .. PlayerData("totalSkins") .. "\n" .. "skin networth: $" .. PlayerData("skinNetworth");
				else
					return 'unavailable'
				end
			end
		end);

			if ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild('devv') then
				return 'money-printer: '..PlayerData('totalMoneyPrinters').."\nrollie: " .. PlayerData("totalRollies") .. "/$" .. PlayerData("totalAmountRollies") .. "\n" .. "gold-cup: " .. PlayerData("totalGoldCups") .. "/$" .. PlayerData("totalAmountGoldCups") .. "\n" .. "gold-crown: " .. PlayerData("totalGoldCrowns") .. "/$" .. PlayerData("totalAmountGoldCrowns") .. "\n" .. "diamond: " .. PlayerData("totalDiamonds") .. "/$" .. PlayerData("totalAmountDiamonds") .. "\n" .. "diamond-ring: " .. PlayerData("totalDiamondRings") .. "/$" .. PlayerData("totalAmountDiamondRings") .. "\n" .. "diamond-ore: " .. PlayerData("totalDiamondOre") .. "/$" .. PlayerData("totalAmountDiamondOre") .. "\n" .. "void-gem: " .. PlayerData("totalVoidGems") .. "/$" .. PlayerData("totalAmountVoidGems") .. "\n" .. "dark-matter-gem: " .. PlayerData("totalDarkMatterGems") .. "/$" .. PlayerData("totalAmountDarkMatterGems") .. "\n" .. "total: " .. PlayerData("totalRareGems") .. "/$" .. PlayerData("totalAmountRareGems");
			else
				return 'unavailable'

		function getlastban(modID, numshadowbans, shadowbanned_reason, banAt)
			if ((modID ~= nil) and (numshadowbans > 0) and (bannedBy == nil) and (banAt == nil)) then
				getgenv().bannedBy = getLoader("userinfo")._request(modID);
			elseif ((modID ~= nil) and (numshadowbans > 0) and (bannedBy == nil)) then
				return shadowbanned_reason;
			elseif ((modID == nil) and (numshadowbans ~= nil) and (numshadowbans > 0)) then
				return "anti-cheat " .. (shadowbanned_reason or "N/A");
			elseif ((modID == nil) and (numshadowbans == 0)) then
				return "none";
			end
		end
		function getBanActive()
			return (getgenv().isBanActive and "true") or "false";
		end
		getString = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(type)
			local state = getLoader("state");
			if (state and (state.data ~= nil)) then
				if (type == "banlog") then
					return "shadowbanActive: " .. getBanActive() .. "\n" .. "ban-count: " .. (numshadowbans or 0) .. "\n" .. "lastbannedfrom: " .. (getlastban(shadowbanned_by, numshadowbans, shadowbanned_reason, banAT_unix) or "N/A") .. "\n";
				elseif (type == "realbanlog") then
					return "shadowbanActive: " .. getBanActive() .. "\n" .. "ban-count: " .. numshadowbans .. "\n" .. "bannedfrom: " .. getlastban(shadowbanned_by, numshadowbans, shadowbanned_reason, banAT_unix) .. "\n" .. "timeLeft: " .. GetBanTimeRemaining();
				end
			else
				return "unavailable";
			end
		end);
		WaitForRootPart = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			if (lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
				return lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
			else
				repeat
					task.wait();
				until lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") 
				return lp.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
			end
		end)
		function FlyInstances()
			if (isFlying == true) then
				if (not playerHumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("VelocityHandler") and not playerHumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("GyroHandler")) then
					if (isFlyActive == true) then
						local bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity");
						bv.Name = "VelocityHandler";
						bv:SetAttribute("whitelist", true);
						bv.Parent = WaitForRootPart();
						bv.MaxForce = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
						bv.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
						local bg = Instance.new("BodyGyro");
						bg.Name = "GyroHandler";
						bg:SetAttribute("whitelist", true);
						bg.Parent = WaitForRootPart();
						bg.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(8999999488, 8999999488, 8999999488);
						bg.P = 1000;
						bg.D = 50;
					else
						removeFlyInstances();
					end
				end
			end
		end

		local currentVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
		local acceleration = 0.2
		local deceleration = 0.2

		Flying = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			local speed = flyspeed or WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get("flyspeed", true) or 200;
			local FlyIsOn = isFlyActive;
			
			if (playerCharacter and playerHumanoid and playerHumanoidRootPart and playerHumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("GyroHandler") and playerHumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("VelocityHandler")) then
				if FlyIsOn then
					NoClipFunc();
					playerHumanoid.PlatformStand = true;
					playerHumanoidRootPart.GyroHandler.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(8999999488, 8999999488, 8999999488);
					playerHumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.MaxForce = Vector3.new(8999999488, 8999999488, 8999999488);
				elseif (FlyIsOn == false) then
					playerHumanoid.PlatformStand = false;
					playerHumanoidRootPart.GyroHandler.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
					playerHumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.MaxForce = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
					currentVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
					return;
				end
				if (FlyIsOn == true) then
					playerHumanoidRootPart.GyroHandler.CFrame = camera.CoordinateFrame;
					local direction = GetMoveVector()
					local desiredVelocity = Vector3.new()
					if (direction.X > 0) then
						desiredVelocity = desiredVelocity + (camera.CFrame.RightVector * direction.X * speed)
					end
					if (direction.X < 0) then
						desiredVelocity = desiredVelocity + (camera.CFrame.RightVector * direction.X * speed)
					end
					if (direction.Z > 0) then
						desiredVelocity = desiredVelocity - (camera.CFrame.LookVector * direction.Z * speed)
					end
					if (direction.Z < 0) then
						desiredVelocity = desiredVelocity - (camera.CFrame.LookVector * direction.Z * speed)
					end					
					if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.Space) then
						desiredVelocity = desiredVelocity + Vector3.new(0, speed, 0)
					end
					if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift) then
						desiredVelocity = desiredVelocity + Vector3.new(0, -speed, 0)
					end					
					if desiredVelocity.Magnitude > 0 then
						currentVelocity = currentVelocity:Lerp(desiredVelocity, acceleration)
					else
						currentVelocity = currentVelocity:Lerp(Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), deceleration)
					end					
					playerHumanoidRootPart.VelocityHandler.Velocity = currentVelocity
				end
			else
				currentVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
			end
		end)

		function NoClipFunc()
			if (loadU:GetConnection("NoClipping") == false) then
				loadU:CreateConnection("NoClipping", RunService.Stepped:Connect(NoClipOn))--function()
					--local result, _ = pcall(NoClipOn);
					-- if (result == false) then
					-- 	__loadNow['sendErrorLog'](getError(result, _),LPH_LINE);
					-- 	loadU:CleanConnectionIf("NoClipping", result);
					-- 	result = nil;
					-- end
				--end));
			end
		end
		NoClipOn = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			if ((isFlyActive == false) and (loadU:GetConnection("NoClipping") ~= false)) then
				loadU:CleanConnection("NoClipping");
				local lpart = {"HumanoidRootPart","UpperTorso","LowerTorso"};
				for _, child in next, playerCharacter:GetDescendants() do
					if (child:IsA("BasePart") and (child.Name == table.find(lpart, child.Name))) then
						child = _partCache.parts[child.Name];
					end
				end
			end
			if (isFlying and (playerCharacter ~= nil)) then
				for _, child in next, playerCharacter:GetDescendants() do
					if (child:IsA("BasePart") and (child.CanCollide == true) and (_partCache.parts[child.Name] == nil)) then
						_partCache:add(child, child.Name);
					end
					if (child:IsA("BasePart") and (child.CanCollide == true)) then
						child.CanCollide = false;
					end
				end
			elseif ((isFlying == false) and (playerCharacter ~= nil)) then
				local lpart = {"HumanoidRootPart","UpperTorso","LowerTorso"};
				for _, child in next, playerCharacter:GetDescendants() do
					if (child:IsA("BasePart") and (child.Name == table.find(lpart, child.Name))) then
						child = _partCache.parts[child.Name];
					end
				end
			end
		end)
		function stopFlyIf(vl)
			if (vl == nil) then
				if (isFlyActive == true) then
					isFlyActive = false;
					NoClipOn();
					if (playerHumanoid.PlatformStand == true) then
						playerHumanoid.PlatformStand = false;
					end
				end
			elseif (vl == true) then
				local lpart = {"HumanoidRootPart","UpperTorso","LowerTorso"};
				for _, child in next, playerCharacter:GetDescendants() do
					if (child:IsA("BasePart") and (child.Name == table.find(lpart, child.Name)) and (_partCache.parts[child.Name] ~= nil)) then
						child = _partCache.parts[child.Name];
					end
				end
			end
		end
		function removeFlyInstances()
			if playerHumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("VelocityHandler") then
				playerHumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("VelocityHandler"):Destroy();
			end
			if playerHumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("GyroHandler") then
				playerHumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("GyroHandler"):Destroy();
			end
		end
		function OnHumanoidFreeFalling(Active)
			local Falling = Active;
			while antiVoid and Falling do
				if (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position.Y <= -200) then
					playerHumanoidRootPart.Anchored = true;
					task.wait(0.6);
					local Success, Error = pcall(function()
						for i, v in pairs(playerCharacter:GetDescendants()) do
							if v:IsA("BasePart") then
								v.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
							end
						end
						playerCharacter:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(1459.2672119140625, 41.2963752746582, -342.5706481933594));
					end);
					if Success then
						playerHumanoidRootPart.Anchored = false;
					end
				end
				task.wait(0.1);
			end
		end
		function tpwalkselection()
			if (seltpwallkselected == nil) then
				return playerHumanoid.MoveDirection;
			elseif (seltpwallkselected() ~= nil) then
				return seltpwallkselected();
			end
		end
		tpwalking = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(delta)
			local tpwalkvaluefunc = tpwalkspeed or WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get("tpwalkspeed", true) or 3.5;
			if (tpwalkIsActive and playerCharacter and playerHumanoid and playerHumanoidRootPart) then
				playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame = playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame + (tpwalkselection() * tpwalkvaluefunc * delta * 10);
				playerHumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = true;
			end
		end)
		function getTPWalkMode()
			local tpwalkerscache = {};
			local tpwalkers = {["Camera LookVector"]=LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
				return Workspace.Camera.CFrame.LookVector;
			end),MoveDirection=LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
				return playerHumanoid.MoveDirection;
			end)};
			for l, v in next, tpwalkers do
				table.insert(tpwalkerscache, l);
			end
			return tpwalkers, tpwalkerscache;
		end
		function SetESPConnections()
			loadU:CreateConnection("ESPAdd", players.PlayerAdded:Connect(LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(player)
				if (player ~= lp) then
					local result, _ = pcall(function()
						ESP_MOD.createEsp(player);
					end);
					if (result == false) then
						__loadNow['sendErrorLog'](getError(result, _),LPH_LINE);
						loadU:CleanConnectionIf("ESPAdd", result);
					end
				end
			end)));
			loadU:CreateConnection("ESPRemove", players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(player)
				local result, _ = pcall(function()
					ESP_MOD.removeEsp(player);
				end);
				if (result == false) then
					__loadNow['sendErrorLog'](getError(result, _),LPH_LINE);
					loadU:CleanConnectionIf("ESPRemove", result);
				end
			end)));
			loadU:CreateConnection("updateESP", RunService.PreRender:Connect(LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
				local result, _ = pcall(function()
					ESP_MOD.updateEsp(getPlayerClosestToFOV);
				end);
				if (result == false) then
					CleanESPConnections()
					__loadNow.sendErrorLog(getError(result, _),LPH_LINE);
					v084('warn')(result,_)
					ESP_MOD.SetESP();
					SetESPConnections();
				end
			end)));
		end
		function CleanESPConnections()
			loadU:CleanConnection("ESPAdd");
			loadU:CleanConnection("ESPRemove");
			loadU:CleanConnection("updateESP");
			-- for l, v in next, players:GetPlayers() do
			-- 	if ESP_MOD.ESPcache[v] then
			-- 		ESP_MOD.removeEsp(v);
			-- 		ESP_MOD.ESPcache[v] = nil;
			-- 	end
			-- end
    		for player, _ in pairs(ESP_MOD.ESPcache) do
				ESP_MOD.removeEsp(player)
				ESP_MOD.ESPcache[player] = nil
			end
		end
		function playAnimation(V1)
			v44 = playerHumanoid;
			v45 = v44 and v44:FindFirstChild("Animator");
			if not v45 then
				return;
			else
				v46 = getLoader("animLoader") and getLoader("animLoader").Get and getLoader("animLoader").Get(V1);
				if not v46 then
					return;
				else
					v45:LoadAnimation(v46):Play();
					return v45:LoadAnimation(v46);
				end
			end
		end
		function checkPlayerHealth()
			local character = playerCharacter or lp.CharacterAdded:Wait();
			local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
			if not humanoid then
				return false, 0;
			end
			return humanoid.Health <= 0, humanoid.Health;
		end

		-- 	if (lp:GetAttribute("isSpawned") and (lp:GetAttribute("isSpawned") == true)) then
		-- 		lp:SetAttribute("isSpawned", false);
		-- 	end

		local MIN_PLAYERS = 15
		local MAX_RETRIES = 7
		local RETRY_DELAY = 10 
		local API_DELAY = 3 
		local SERVER_ATTEMPT_DELAY = 2 
		local Folder = "TeTraX.IO"
		local File = Folder.."/servercache"
		local VisitedFile = Folder.."/visitedalready" 
		local ErrorLogFile = Folder.."/teleport_errors.log"
		local http = v084('http_request') or v084('request')
		if not http then
			error("No compatible HTTP request function found")
		end

		function serverHop()
			local readfile = v084('readfile')
			local function jsone(str) return HttpService:JSONEncode(str) end
			local function jsond(str) return HttpService:JSONDecode(str) end
			if not v084('isfolder')(Folder) then
				v084('makefolder')(Folder)
			end
			if not v084('isfile')(File) then
				v084('writefile')(File, jsone({servers = {}, timestamp = 0}))
			end
			if not v084('isfile')(VisitedFile) then
				v084('writefile')(VisitedFile, jsone({visited = {}}))
			end
			if not v084('isfile')(ErrorLogFile) then
				v084('writefile')(ErrorLogFile, "Teleport Error Log:\n")
			end
			local function logError(message)
				local timestamp = os.date("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
				pcall(function()
					appendfile(ErrorLogFile, string.format("[%s] %s\n", timestamp, message))
				end)
			end

			local function loadVisitedServers()
				local success, data = pcall(function()
					local content = v084('readfile')(VisitedFile)
					return jsond(content)
				end)
				if not success or type(data) ~= "table" then
					v084('writefile')(VisitedFile, jsone({visited = {}}))
					return {}
				end
				return data.visited or {}
			end

			local function saveVisitedServer(jobId)
				local visited = loadVisitedServers()
				table.insert(visited, jobId)
				pcall(function()
					v084('writefile')(VisitedFile, jsone({visited = visited}))
				end)
			end

			local function isServerVisited(jobId)
				local visited = loadVisitedServers()
				for _, id in ipairs(visited) do
					if id == jobId then
						return true
					end
				end
				return false
			end

			local function fetchServers(placeId, maxRetries)
				maxRetries = maxRetries or 5
				local retryCount = 0
				local lastError = nil
				local serverData = nil
				task.wait(API_DELAY)
				while retryCount < maxRetries and not serverData do
					local success, response = pcall(function()
						return http({
							Url = string.format("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/%s/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100", placeId),
							Method = "GET"
						})
					end)
					if not success then
						lastError = "HTTP request failed: " .. response
						retryCount = retryCount + 1
						task.wait(1)
					else
						if response.StatusCode ~= 200 then
							lastError = "HTTP " .. response and response.StatusCode or response
							retryCount = retryCount + 1
							task.wait(1)
						else
							local jsonSuccess, body = pcall(jsond, response.Body)
							if not jsonSuccess then
								lastError = "JSON decode failed: " .. body
								retryCount = retryCount + 1
								task.wait(1)
							else
								if not body.data then
									lastError = "No server data in response"
									retryCount = retryCount + 1
									task.wait(1)
								else
									serverData = body.data
								end
							end
						end
					end
				end
				if not serverData then
					error("Failed to fetch servers after " .. maxRetries .. " attempts. Last error: " .. (lastError or "unknown"))
				end
				return serverData
			end
			local function getData()
				local servers = {}
				local placeId = game.PlaceId
				if v084('isfile')(File) then
					local success, cached = pcall(function()
						return jsond(v084('readfile')(File))
					end)
					if success and cached and cached.servers and cached.timestamp then
						if os.time() - cached.timestamp < 300 then -- 5 minute cache
							return cached.servers
						end
					end
				end
				local serverData = fetchServers(placeId)
				for _, v in ipairs(serverData) do
					if v.playing and v.playing >= MIN_PLAYERS then

						table.insert(servers, v)

					end
				end
				pcall(function()
					v084('writefile')(File, jsone({
						servers = servers,
						timestamp = os.time()
					}))
				end)
				return servers
			end

			local function safeTeleport(serverId)
				local success, err = pcall(function()
					local teleportFailed = false
					local teleportFailedConnection
					teleportFailedConnection = TeleportService.TeleportInitFailed:Connect(function(player, teleportResult, errorMessage)
						teleportFailed = true
						local msg = string.format("Teleport failed to %s: %s (%s)", serverId, tostring(errorMessage), tostring(teleportResult))
						logError(msg)
						teleportFailedConnection:Disconnect()
					end)
					TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, serverId, lp)
					if not teleportFailed then
						WindUI.saveDataSettings:LoadDataIf('ignoreTranslation',true)
						--lp:Kick(adminDetected == false and "SERVER HOPPING..." or typeof(adminDetected) == 'table' and adminDetected.name ~= nil and 'admin detected server hopping...'..'\nname: '..adminDetected.name)
					end
					local startTime = os.clock()
					while os.clock() - startTime < 5 and not teleportFailed do
						task.wait(0.1)
					end
					if teleportFailed then
						error("Teleport failed (handled by event)")
					end
				end)
				if not success then
					logError(string.format("Teleport attempt to %s failed: %s", serverId, err))
					return false, err
				end
				return true
			end

			local function clearVisitedCache()
				pcall(function()
					v084('writefile')(VisitedFile, jsone({visited = {}}))
				end)
			end

			local function attemptServerHop(attemptNumber)
				attemptNumber = attemptNumber or 1
				local servers = getData()
				if #servers == 0 then
					return false
				end

				if game.JobId ~= "" then
					saveVisitedServer(game.JobId)
				end
				local teleportAttempted = false
				local attemptedServers = 0
				for _, server in ipairs(servers) do
					if not isServerVisited(server.id) and (server.playing or 0) > 0 then
						attemptedServers = attemptedServers + 1
						local success, err = safeTeleport(server.id)
						if success then
							teleportAttempted = true
							break
						else
							task.wait(SERVER_ATTEMPT_DELAY)
						end
					end
				end
				if not teleportAttempted then
					clearVisitedCache()
					servers = getData()
					for _, server in ipairs(servers) do
						if (server.playing or 0) > 0 then
							attemptedServers = attemptedServers + 1
							
							local success, err = safeTeleport(server.id)
							if success then
								teleportAttempted = true
								break
							else
								task.wait(SERVER_ATTEMPT_DELAY)
							end
						end
					end
				end
				if not teleportAttempted and attemptNumber < MAX_RETRIES then
					task.wait(RETRY_DELAY)
					return attemptServerHop(attemptNumber + 1)
				end
				return teleportAttempted
			end
			local success = attemptServerHop(1)
			if not success then
				local servers = getData()
				if #servers > 0 then
					local randomServer = servers[math.random(1, #servers)]
					safeTeleport(randomServer.id)
					task.wait(5)
				end
			end
			return success
		end
		function getAdmins()
			local admins = {}--9741804919}
			local specialroles = getLoader("specialroles")
			if not specialroles then return admins end
			
			local roles = {"heros", "admins", "developer"}
			
			for _, role in ipairs(roles) do
				if specialroles[role] and specialroles[role].users then
					for _, user in next, specialroles[role].users do
						if user > 3 and not table.find(admins, user) then
							table.insert(admins, user)
						end
					end
				end
			end
			return admins
		end
		local adminchecker = getAdmins();

		if (antiAdminMode == nil) then
			local v0 = WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get("antiadminMode",true) or 'kick';
			getgenv().antiAdminMode = v0;
			v0 = nil;
		end
		if (antiAdmin == nil) then
			local v0 = WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get("antiadmin");
			getgenv().antiAdmin = v0;
			v0 = nil;
		end
		function kickOnAdminJoin(plr)
			if ((plr.UserId == adminchecker[table.find(adminchecker, plr.UserId)]) and (plr.UserId ~= lpuserid) and (antiAdmin == true)) then
				manager:KillAll()
				task.wait(.1)
				TeleportToRandomSpawn()
				pcall(function()
					__loadNow['sendAdminAlert']({
						id = plr.UserId,
						user = plr.Name
					})
				end)
				adminDetected = true
				local kickmsg = antiAdminMode ~= 'serverhop' and "[TETRAX-KICK]" .. "\n" .. "[ADMIN]: " .. plr.Name .. "\n" .. "You have been kicked because TeTraX found a admin in the current server!" or antiAdminMode == 'serverhop' and "[TETRAX-KICK]" .. "\n" .. "[ADMIN]: " .. plr.Name .. "\n" .. "switching servers because TeTraX found a admin in the current server!";
				lp:Kick(kickmsg);
				wait()
				if antiAdminMode == 'serverhop' then
					serverHop()
				end
			end
		end


		if (antiAdmin == true) then
			for l, v in next, players:GetPlayers() do
				kickOnAdminJoin(v);
			end
		end

			if (forceNotFriends == true) then

				return lp:IsFriendsWith(userId);
			end
		end)

				elseif (forcefists == true) then

			elseif (boot == true) then
				local _, result, guid = pcall(function()
					local _, guidd = v3item.inventory and v3item.inventory.getEquippedItem();
					return _, guidd;
				end);

		function equip(item)
			if typeof(item) == 'boolean' then
				return
			end
			local signal = getLoader('Signal')
			local exec = string.find(v084('identifyexecutor')(), "Delta")
			local v3item = not exec and clientRequire(ReplicatedStorage.devv).load('v3item') or getLoader('v3item')
			if (item ~= nil) then
				-- local result, _ = pcall(function()
					v3item.inventory.setEquipped(item);
					if not exec then
						setidentity(mainIdentity)
					end
				-- end);
			elseif (item == nil) then
				local inv = v3item.inventory and v3item.inventory.unequipAll
				inv()
			end

		end

		function refreshdistance(v)
			if v.Character then
				return (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position - v.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude;
			else
				return (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position - v.Position).Magnitude;
			end
		end
		function GetPlayerEquipped(plr)
			if ((plr ~= nil) and getLoader("state").equipped and getLoader("state").equipped[plr.UserId]) then
				return getLoader("state").equipped[plr.UserId];
			end
		end
		local characterParts = {};
		local HITBOX_MULTIPLIERS = {Head=5,UpperTorso=4,LowerTorso=4,HumanoidRootPart=6,LeftUpperArm=3,RightUpperArm=3,LeftUpperLeg=3,RightUpperLeg=3};
		function updateCharacterParts()
            table.clear(characterParts)
            if not playerCharacter then
				return;
			end
			for partName, multiplier in pairs(HITBOX_MULTIPLIERS) do
				local part = playerCharacter:FindFirstChild(partName);
				if (part and part:IsA("BasePart")) then
					table.insert(characterParts, {Part=part,Size=(part.Size * multiplier)});
				end
			end
		end
		updateCharacterParts();
		function isPlayerAlive(player)
			if (not player or not player.Character) then
				return false;
			end
			local humanoid = player.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
			return humanoid and (humanoid.Health > 0);
		end

		function ifisKnocked() 
			local clientrep = getLoader('ClientReplicator')
			local isKnocked =clientrep and clientrep.Get(lp,'knocked')
			if clientrep and isKnocked == true then
				return CFrame.new(0,-20,0)
			end
			return CFrame.new(0,0,8)
		end
		attackUntilDead = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(enemyPlayer)
			local clientr = getLoader('ClientReplicator')
			local v3i =getLoader('v3item')
			if not isPlayerAlive(enemyPlayer) then
				return false;
			end
			local enemyRootPart = enemyPlayer.Character and enemyPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
			if (not playerHumanoidRootPart or not enemyRootPart) then
				return false;
			end
			if checkedAIMKILLING == true then
				return
			end
			local result;
			local oldItemf = v3i.inventory and v3i.inventory.getEquippedItem()
			local oldPos = playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame
			local fists,name = getItemGUID(false,'Fists')
			repeat
				getgenv().checkedAIMKILLING = true;
				result = pcall(function()
					CFrameTP(enemyRootPart.CFrame * ifisKnocked())--CFrame.new(0, 0, 7);
					equip(fists)
					FireServer("attackMeleeHit", unpack({[1]="player",[2]={meleeType="meleemegapunch",hitPlayerId=enemyPlayer.UserId}}));
					if clientr.Get(enemyPlayer,'knocked') then
						FireServer("finish", enemyPlayer);
					end
					RunService.Heartbeat:Wait();
				end);
				if not result then
					__loadNow['sendErrorLog'](getError(result, _),LPH_LINE);
				end
			until (result == false)  or (isPlayerAlive(enemyPlayer) ~= true) or not playerHumanoidRootPart or (playerHumanoid.Health < 1) or antiAimOnMe == false
			getgenv().checkedAIMKILLING= false;
			CFrameTP(oldPos)
			equip(oldItemf)
			return true;
		end)
		checkAimAtMe = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(otherPlayer)
			if (otherPlayer == lp) then
				return;
			end
			if not isPlayerAlive(otherPlayer) then
				return;
			end
			local aimPoint = getLoader("ClientReplicator").Get(otherPlayer, "aimPoint");
			if not aimPoint then
				return;
			end
			for _, partData in next, characterParts do
				local relativePoint = partData.Part.CFrame:PointToObjectSpace(aimPoint);
				local halfSize = partData.Size / 2;
				if ((math.abs(relativePoint.X) <= halfSize.X) and (math.abs(relativePoint.Y) <= halfSize.Y) and (math.abs(relativePoint.Z) <= halfSize.Z)) then
					attackUntilDead(otherPlayer);
					return;
				end
			end
		end)
		getItemGUID =LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(multi, name)
			local inventory = getLoader("v3item").inventory and getLoader("v3item").inventory.currentItemsData;
			if inventory then
				if (multi == true) then
					for l, v in next, inventory do
						if (not v.isStashed and (v.name == name[table.find(name, v.name)])) then
							return v.guid, v.name;
						end
					end
				else
					for l, v in next, inventory do
						if (not v.isStashed and (v.name == name)) then
							return v.guid, v.name;
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end)
		function getItemPrice(item)
			local gitemz = getLoader("v3items") and getLoader("v3items").items;
			if gitemz then
				if (getLoader("v3items").items[item] and getLoader("v3items").items[item].data.cost) then
					return getLoader("v3items").items[item].data.cost;
				end
			else
				return 0;
			end
		end
		function getVests()
			local armorcache = {};
			local v3items = getLoader("v3items") and getLoader("v3items").items;
			if v3items then
				for l, v in next, v3items do
					if string.find(l, "Vest") then
						table.insert(armorcache, l);
					end
				end
			end
			return armorcache;
		end

		CanPurchase = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(item)
			local itemPrice = item and getItemPrice(item);
			if (itemPrice and (getItemPrice(item) < getPlayerCash())) then
				return true;
			else
				return false;
			end
		end)

		function getSellPrice(f)
			local items = getLoader('v3items').items
			for l,v in next,items do
				if v.data and v.data.name == f and v.data.sellPrice then
					return v.data.sellPrice
				end
			end
		end

		validateSell = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(s)
			local total =0
			local f = getLoader('v3item').inventory.get(s)
			if f ~= nil then
				local amount = f and f.ammoManager and f.ammoManager.ammo or f.ammo
				local price = getSellPrice(f.name)
				if f.type ~= 'Gun' and amount > 1 then
					total = total + price * amount
				elseif f.type ~= 'Gun' and amount == 1 then
					total = total + price
				elseif f.type == 'Gun' then
					total = price
				end
			end
			return total
		end)

		buyItem = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(item)
			local itemD = ItemCheck();
			if (item and not itemD[table.find(itemD, item)] and (CanPurchase(item) == true) and (getTotalSlotsUsed() < 32)) then
				return InvokeServer("attemptPurchase", item);
			end
			return false
		end)

			end
		end

			end
		end
		function stopAnimations(anim)
			local v4 = playerCharacter;
			local v5 = v4 and v4:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
			local v6 = v5 and v5:FindFirstChild("Animator");
			if not v6 then
				return;
			else
				for _, v8 in ipairs(v6:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
					if ((typeof(anim) == "Instance") and (v8.Name == anim.Name)) then
						v8:Stop(0);
					elseif (v8.Name == anim) then
						v8:Stop(0);
					end
				end
				return;
			end
		end
		local gunkillers = {"Raygun","M249 SAW","M4A1","AK-47","Deagle",'Scar L','AUG','M1 Garand','Minigun'}

		local bladekillsettings = {
			currentGUID = nil,
			throwStickyCooldown =85 ,

		function throwSticky(guid, blade, item, vec1, vec2)
			local equipped = item
			local signal = getLoader('Signal')
			local c0, c1 = signal.InvokeServer('throwSticky', guid, blade, item.guid, vec1, vec2)
			local v68 = equipped and equipped.ammoManager
			if v68 ~= nil then
				if v68.ammo ~= nil and v68.ammo == 0 then
					signal.FireServer('removeItem', equipped.guid)
				elseif v68 and v68.ammo and v68.ammo >= 1 then
					v68:setAmmo((v68.ammo - (equipped.numProjectiles or 1)))
				end
			end
			return c0, c1
		end

		function hitSticky(returnedguid, hitpart, CFrame1, CFrame2)
			local signal = getLoader('Signal')
			signal.InvokeServer('hitSticky', returnedguid, hitpart, CFrame1, CFrame2)
		end		
		function createDiedListenerForAnimations(hum)
			loadU:CreateConnection("AnimationButtonResetListener", hum.Died:Connect(function()
				if (z001.main.animationStop ~= nil) then
					if (typeof(z001.main.animationStop) == "table") then
						if (z001.main.animationStop.UIElements ~= nil) then
							for l, v in next, z001.main.animationStop.UIElements do
								v:Destroy();
								z001.main.animationStop.UIElements = nil;
							end
							for l, v in next, z001.main.animationStop.ButtonFrame.UIElements do
								v:Destroy();
								v = nil;
							end
							loadU:CleanConnection("AnimationButtonResetListener");
							getgenv().selectedanimation = nil;
							z001.main.animationStop = nil;
						end
					end
					z001.main.animationStop = nil;
					getgenv().selectedanimation = nil;
					loadU:CleanConnection("AnimationButtonResetListener");
				else
					getgenv().selectedanimation = nil;
					loadU:CleanConnection("AnimationButtonResetListener");
				end
			end));
		end

		function getTotalSlotsUsed()
			local rr = 0;
			for l, v in next, getLoader("v3item").inventory.currentItemsData do
				if not v.isStashed then
					rr = rr + 1;
				end
			end
			return rr;
		end
		function knockPlr(v)
			if (v.Character and not v.Character:FindFirstChild("ForceField") and v.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")) then
				local chr = v.Character;
				local hum = v.Character.Humanoid;
				local root = v.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
				local isKnocked = getLoader('ClientReplicator').Get(v,'knocked')
				local shouldAttack = canAttackPlayer(v)
				if shouldAttack and not isKnocked and not checkFriendship(v.UserId, DamageFriends or false) and v.Name ~= lpname then

					meleeItemHit({[1]="player",[2]={meleeType="meleemegapunch",hitPlayerId=v.UserId}});
				end
			end
		end
		function bladeKillPlr(v,bladeKind)

			local bladekind = bladeKind or selectedBladeSingle or 'Ninja Star'
			local load = getLoader
			local guid = load('GUID')
			local inventory = load('v3item').inventory
			local blade =inventory.getFromName(bladekind)
			local equipped= inventory.getEquippedItem()
			if blade == nil and getTotalSlotsUsed() < 32 then
				buyItem(bladekind)
				blade =inventory.getFromName(bladekind)
			end
			if blade ~= nil and v ~= nil then									
				local lpRighthand = playerCharacter and playerCharacter:FindFirstChild('RightHand')						
				local chr = v.Character
				local root = chr and chr:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')
				local humanoid = chr and chr:FindFirstChild('Humanoid')
				local head = chr and chr:FindFirstChild('Head')
				local isFriend = checkFriendship(v.UserId, DamageFriends or false)			
				if v ~= lp and lpRighthand and not isFriend and canAttackPlayer(v) and chr and root and head and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 and playerCharacter and playerHumanoidRootPart then
					local distance = (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position - root.Position).Magnitude
					local targetPos = root.Position                            
					local throwOrigin = lpRighthand.Position
					local direction = (targetPos - throwOrigin).Unit
					local speed = math.huge
					local velocityVector = direction * speed
					local v68 = blade and blade.ammoManager
					if v68 ~= nil and (v68.ammoOut ~= nil) and (v68.ammoOut < 3) then
						local amount = (5 - v68.ammoOut)
						for i = 1, amount do
							buyAmmo(blade.name)
						end
					end
					local currentTime = os.time()
					if bladekillsettings.currentGUID == nil or (currentTime - bladekillsettings.lastThrowTime) >= bladekillsettings.throwStickyCooldown then
						if blade then
							equip(blade.guid)
							local calledguid = guid()
							bladekillsettings.otherArg, bladekillsettings.currentGUID = throwSticky(calledguid, bladekind, blade, velocityVector,targetPos)--vector.create(9e9,9e9,9e9),vector.create(9e9,9e9,9e9))-- vector.create(0,0,0))
							bladekillsettings.lastThrowTime = currentTime
							if blade and blade.SetEquipped then
								blade:SetEquipped(false)
							end							
							inventory.unequipAll()
						end
					end
					task.spawn(function()
						local thrownObjectCFrame = CFrame.new(targetPos, targetPos + direction)  
						local hitPart = v.Character and v.Character:FindFirstChild('Head')
						if hitPart then
							local offsetCFrame = thrownObjectCFrame:toObjectSpace(hitPart.CFrame)
							local currentCFrame = thrownObjectCFrame
							hitSticky(bladekillsettings.currentGUID, head, offsetCFrame, currentCFrame)
						end
					end)
				end
			end


			-- local bladekind = selectedBladeSingle or 'Ninja Star'
			-- local load = getLoader
			-- local guid = load('GUID')
			-- local inventory = load('v3item').inventory
			-- local blade =inventory.getFromName(bladekind)
			-- local equipped= inventory.getEquippedItem()
			-- if blade == nil and getTotalSlotsUsed() < 32 then
			-- 	buyItem(bladekind)

			-- end

			-- 	local lpRighthand = playerCharacter and playerCharacter:FindFirstChild('RightHand')

			-- 	local root = chr and chr:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')

			-- 		local distance = (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position - root.Position).Magnitude

		function isSellable(item)
			if (getLoader("v3items").items[item] and getLoader("v3items").items[item].data.sellPrice) then
				return true;
			else
				return false;
			end
		end

			loadU:CreateConnection("antiSitConnection", hum.StateChanged:Connect(function(v, c)
				if ((antiSit == true) and (c == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated)) then
					hum:ChangeState("Running");
				end
			end));
		end

			loadU:CreateConnection("antiSitHumanoidConnection", hum.Died:Connect(function()
				loadU:CleanConnection("antiSitConnection");

		end

			if (localChar and localChar:WaitForChild("Humanoid")) then
				if (loadU:GetConnection("antiSitHumanoidConnection") == false) then
					antiSitFuncHum(localChar.Humanoid);
					antiSitFunc(localChar.Humanoid);
				else
					loadU:CleanConnection("antiSitHumanoidConnection");
					antiSitFuncHum(localChar.Humanoid);
					antiSitFunc(localChar.Humanoid);
				end
			end
		end));
		SetHumanoidEnabled = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(v41, v42, v43)

			if v43 then
				return;
			else
				local v44 = v41.Character;
				local v45 = v44 and v44:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
				if not v45 then
					return;
				else
					local v46 = v44:FindFirstChild("Animate");
					if v46 then
						v46.Enabled = v42;
					end
					-- for v47, v48 in ipairs(v45:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
					-- 	v48:Stop(0);
					-- end
					for v49, v50 in pairs(Enum.HumanoidStateType:GetEnumItems()) do
						if ((v50 ~= Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics) and (v50 ~= Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead) and (v50 ~= Enum.HumanoidStateType.None) and (v50 ~= Enum.HumanoidStateType.RunningNoPhysics) and (v50 ~= Enum.HumanoidStateType.StrafingNoPhysics)) then
							v45:SetStateEnabled(v50, v42);
						end
					end
					v45:ChangeState((v42 and Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp) or Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics);
					return;
				end
			end
		end)
		TweenTeleport = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(cframe, speed, tweenfunc)
			if adminDetected then return end
			local ts = TweenService;
			local part = playerHumanoidRootPart;
			local ti = TweenInfo.new(speed, tweenfunc);
			local tp = {CFrame=cframe};
			local tstime = ts:Create(part, ti, tp);
			return tstime;
		end)
		function disableGrabAttempt()
			local signal = lp:GetAttributeChangedSignal("grabbedBy");
			local signal2 = lp:GetAttributeChangedSignal("struggling");
			local connections = v084('getconnections')(signal);
			local conn = v084('getconnections')(signal2);
			for l, v in next, connections do
				v:Disable();
				v = nil;
			end
			for l, v in next, conn do
				v:Disable();
				v = nil;
			end
			local t
			local grabPlayer = v084('getupvalue')(getLoader("Signal").InvokeServer, 1)['grabPlayer'];
			if grabPlayer and grabPlayer.OnClientEvent then
				for l,v in next,v084('getconnections')(grabPlayer.OnClientEvent) do
					v:Disable();
				end				
			end

			local fling = v084('getupvalue')(getLoader("Signal").InvokeServer, 1)['flingPlayer'];
			if fling and fling.OnClientEvent then
				for l,v in next,v084('getconnections')(fling.OnClientEvent) do
					v:Disable();
				end
			end
			local teleport = v084('getupvalue')(getLoader("Signal").InvokeServer, 1)['teleport'];
			if teleport and teleport.OnClientEvent then
				for l,v in next,v084('getconnections')(teleport.OnClientEvent) do
					v:Disable();
				end
			end
			getLoader('Signal').LinkSignal('teleport',function(cframe)
				if UseCustomSpawnPoint == true and spawnPointCFrame ~= nil then
				    if lp and lp.Character and lp.Character.PrimaryPart then
						lp.Character:PivotTo(spawnPointCFrame)
					end
				else
				    if lp and lp.Character and lp.Character.PrimaryPart then
						lp.Character:PivotTo(cframe)
					end
				end
			end)
		end
		if getLoader('Signal').InvokeServer ~= nil then
			disableGrabAttempt();
		end

		calculateReplicationCFrame =LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(targetLockPoint, itemData, gunModel)
			if not gunModel or not gunModel.PrimaryPart then return end
			local muzzle = gunModel.PrimaryPart:FindFirstChild('Muzzle')
			if muzzle then
				local muzzlePos = muzzle.WorldCFrame.Position    
				local direction = (targetLockPoint - muzzlePos).Unit
				local bulletCFrame = CFrame.new(muzzlePos, muzzlePos + direction)
				return bulletCFrame
			end
		end)

		function getfovradius()
			if ffovcircle
			and ffovcircle.Radius then
				v1 = getgenv().ffovcircle.Radius or 20
			else
				v1 = 20
			end
			return v1
		end
		getPlayerClosestToFOV = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			targetFOVHIT = nil
			local maxDist = math.huge
			for _,v in next,players:GetPlayers() do
				if v.Name ~= lpname and not checkFriendship(v.UserId, DamageFriends or false) and not table.find(nokill,v.Name) and v.Character and not v.Character:FindFirstChild("ForceField") and v.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") and v.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid").Health ~= 0 then
					local pos, vis = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(v.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position)
					local dist
					if pos ~= nil and ffovcircle ~= nil and ffovcircle.Position ~= nil then
						dist = (Vector2.new(ffovcircle.Position.X,ffovcircle.Position.Y) - Vector2.new(pos.X, pos.Y)).magnitude
					end
					if dist ~= nil and dist < maxDist and vis and dist <= getfovradius() then
						local torsoPos = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(v.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position)
						local torsoDist = (Vector2.new(ffovcircle.Position.X, ffovcircle.Position.Y) - Vector2.new(torsoPos.X, torsoPos.Y)).magnitude
						local headPos = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(v.Character.Head.Position)
						local headDist = (Vector2.new(ffovcircle.Position.X, ffovcircle.Position.Y) - Vector2.new(headPos.X, headPos.Y)).magnitude
						if wallCheck then
							if torsoDist > headDist then
								if notBehindWall(v.Character.HumanoidRootPart) then
									targetFOVHIT = v
								end
							else
								if notBehindWall(v.Character.Head) then
									targetFOVHIT = v
								end
							end
						elseif not wallCheck then
							if v.Character.Head then
								targetFOVHIT = v
							end
						end
						maxDist = dist
					end
				end
			end

		function gradient(ab, ac, ad)
			local b = "";
			local e = #ab;
			for g = 1, e do
				local h = (g - 1) / math.max(e - 1, 1);
				local i = math.floor((ac.R + ((ad.R - ac.R) * h)) * 255);
				local j = math.floor((ac.G + ((ad.G - ac.G) * h)) * 255);
				local k = math.floor((ac.B + ((ad.B - ac.B) * h)) * 255);
				local n = ab:sub(g, g);
				b = b .. '<font color=\"rgb(' .. i .. ", " .. j .. ", " .. k .. ')\">' .. n .. "</font>";
			end
			return b;
		end

		function getGoodGuns()
			local rareGuns = {
				'Pulse Rifle',
				'El Fuego',
				'Diamond Banana Peel'
			}
			local goodGuns = {}
			local v0 = getLoader('v3items').items
			for l,v in next,v0 or {} do
				if v.type ~= nil and v.type == 'Gun' and v.data.name ~= nil and v.data.unpurchasable and not table.find(goodGuns,v.data.name) then
					table.insert(goodGuns,v.data.name)
				elseif v.type ~= nil and v.type == 'Gun' and table.find(rareGuns,v.data.name) and not table.find(goodGuns,v.data.name) then
					table.insert(goodGuns,v.data.name)
				end
			end
			return goodGuns
		end

        function removercheck(datav) --
			if autoArmor and datav.name == selectedVest then
				return true
			end
			if autoHeal and datav.name == selectedFoodfunc then
				return true
			end
			local isPlrKillerActive = knifeAura or PlayerActionToggled and selectedplrsmode == 'blade kill' or allPlayerOptionToggledBlades and mainSelectedAllPlayerMode == 'blades'
            local isWeapon = datav.name == 'Tomahawk' or datav.name == 'Ninja Star'
            if isPlrKillerActive and isWeapon then
                return true
			end
			if PlayerActionToggled and selectedplrsmode == 'blade kill' and isWeapon then
				return true
            end
            if utBuy == datav.name then
                return true
            end
            return datav.name == 'RPG' and rpgBotKill == true or selectedGunBot == datav.name and gunKillBot == true or selectedallplrmodeGun == datav.name and allPlayerOptionToggledGuns == true or selectedallplrsinglemodeGun == datav.name and PlayerActionToggled == true 
        end
		local devvGUNS = {}
		function getAllGunTypes()
			local d = ReplicatedStorage.devv.shared.Indicies.v3items.bin.Gun
			if d then
				for l,v in next,d:GetDescendants() do
					if not v:IsDescendantOf(d.subtypes) and v.ClassName ~= 'Folder' then
						devvGUNS[v.Name] = v084('require')(v)
					end
				end
			end
			return devvGUNS
		end


		function isGun(gun)
			return devvGUNS[gun] ~= nil
		end

				function resetDealer()
					tetraxData.dealerData.remainingCooldownSeconds = 0
					tetraxData.dealerData.cash = 50000
					tetraxData.dealerData.isDealerCooldown = false
					tetraxData.dealerData.startedSelling = false
					if z001 and z001.cash and z001.cash.autoSell and z001.cash.autoSell.SetDesc ~= nil then
						task.wait()
						z001.cash.autoSell:SetDesc(nil)
					end
				end
				function stashItem(item)

				end			
				lockerSlots = function()
					return lp:GetAttribute('lockerSlots') or getLoader('globals').DEFAULT_LOCKER_SLOTS

				function getAvailableSlots()
					return (lockerSlots()-getLoader('v3item').inventory.getNumStashed())
				end						
				LinkSignal('makeToast', function(message, k, m)
					if not message:find("dealer", 1, true) then  -- Case-insensitive search
						return  -- Exit if not a dealer message
					end
					local text = message
					local function parseNumber(str)
						if not str then return 0 end
						local cleanStr = str:gsub("[^%d]", "")
						return tonumber(cleanStr) or 0
					end

					local cashStr = text:match("%$(%d[%d,]*)")
					tetraxData.dealerData.cash = parseNumber(cashStr)
					local hours = parseNumber(text:match("(%d+)h"))
					local minutes = parseNumber(text:match("(%d+)m"))
					local totalMinutes = hours * 60 + minutes
					local function minutesToSeconds(minutes)
						minutes = tonumber(minutes) or 0
						return minutes * 60
					end
					tetraxData.dealerData.sec = minutesToSeconds(totalMinutes)

					-- Always start the cooldown timer if there's a valid time
					if tetraxData.dealerData.sec > 0 then
						if loadU:GetConnection('dealerCooldown') ~= false then
							loadU:CleanConnection('dealerCooldown')  -- Clear old connection if it exists
						end
						tetraxData.dealerData.remainingCooldownSeconds = tetraxData.dealerData.sec + 60 -- Start timer immediately
						loadU:CreateConnection('dealerCooldown', RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
							tetraxData.dealerData.remainingCooldownSeconds = tetraxData.dealerData.remainingCooldownSeconds - deltaTime
							if tetraxData.dealerData.remainingCooldownSeconds <= 0 then
								resetDealer()
								loadU:CleanConnection('dealerCooldown')  -- Clean up when done
							end
						end))
					end
					if tetraxData.dealerData.remainingCooldownSeconds <= 0 then
						resetDealer()
						loadU:CleanConnection('dealerCooldown')  -- Clean up when done
					end
					if tetraxData.dealerData.cash <= 300 then
						tetraxData.dealerData.isDealerCooldown = true
					elseif tetraxData.dealerData.cash >300 then
						tetraxData.dealerData.isDealerCooldown = false
					end
				end)

		function securepcall(func,...)
			local args={...}
			local result,_ = pcall(func,unpack(args))
			if not result then
				v084('warn')('[securepcall]',result,_)
			end
		end
		function spcall(func,...)
			local args={...}
			local result,_ = pcall(func)
			if not result then
				v084('warn')('[spcall]',result,_)
			end
		end

		function indexUIObj(name, elem, func)
			local r,p = pcall(function()
				if ((z001[name] == nil) and (elem == false)) then
					z001[name] = func;
				elseif (z001[name] and (z001[name][elem] == nil)) then
					z001[name][elem] = func;
				end
			end)
			if r == false then
				__loadNow.sendErrorLog(r,LPH_LINE)
			end
		end


		function hideObject(tabElem,value,g)
			if tabElem ~= nil then
				for l,v in next,tabElem do 
					if typeof(v) == 'table' and v.UIElements then
						for i,h in next,v.UIElements do
							if i ~= 'Locked' and h.Visible ~= nil and v.Title ~= "TeTraX"then
								h.Visible = value
							end
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end

		function setDesc(tab,elem,msg)
			if z001[tab] and z001[tab][elem] and z001[tab][elem].SetDesc ~= nil then
				z001[tab][elem]:SetDesc(msg)
			end
		end

			function deep_copy(original_table, seen_tables)
				seen_tables = seen_tables or {}
				if typeof(original_table) ~= "table" then
					return original_table
				end
				if seen_tables[original_table] then
					return seen_tables[original_table]
				end
				local new_table = {}
				seen_tables[original_table] = new_table
				for key, value in pairs(original_table) do
					new_table[key] = deep_copy(value, seen_tables)
				end
				return new_table
			end

			function DoesHaveItemAlready(name)

			function canBuyAmmo(v50)
				local xq = getLoader("v3items");
				local v52 = xq and (xq.getItemData ~= nil) and xq.getItemData(v50);
				if (not v52 or not v52.ammo) then
					return false;
				else
					local v599 = getLoader("v3item").inventory.getFromName(v50)
					local v53 = v599 and v599.ammoManager;
					local v54 = v53 and v53.ammoOut;
					local v55 = v52 and v52.maxAmmo;
					local v56 = v52 and v52.ammoPurchaseAmount; 
					local v57 = v52 and v52.isConsumable;
					if not v56 then
						return false;
					else
						if v57 and v56 ~= nil and v55 ~= nil then
							if v53 ~= nil and ((v53.ammo + v56) <= v55) then
								return true;
							end
						elseif v54 ~=nil and v56 ~= nil and v55 ~= nil and ((v54 + v56) <= v55) then
							return true;
						end
						return false;
					end
				end
			end
			function reload(clientrep,v3item,item,equipped)
				local load = getLoader
				local iee = v3item
				local isreloading =clientrep.Get(lp, "reloading")
				local isknocked = clientrep.Get(lp,'knocked')
				if item ~= nil  and isknocked ~= true and equipped ~= nil and equipped.name == item.name then
					local itemGUID = item and item.guid
					if itemGUID ~= nil then
						task.spawn(function()
							clientrep.Set(lp, "reloading", true);
							clientrep.Replicate("reloading");							

							FireServer("reload", itemGUID);
							task.wait(item.reloadTime)
							clientrep.Set(lp, "reloading", false);
						end)
					end
				end
			end

			function getAmmo(ite)
				local v68 = ite
				local v69 = v68 and v68.ammoManager;
				return v69;
			end
			function buyAmmo(name)
				if canBuyAmmo(name) then
					local dd= getLoader('v3items')
					local v63 = dd and dd.getItemData and dd.getItemData(name);
					local v65 = v63.ammoPurchaseAmount;
					local v66, v67 = InvokeServer("attemptPurchaseAmmo", name);
					local v68 = getLoader("v3item").inventory.get(v67);
					local v69 = v68 and v68.ammoManager;
					if v69 then
						if v63.isConsumable then
							v69:setAmmo(v69.ammo + v65);
						else
							v69:setAmmoOut(v69.ammoOut + v65);
						end
					end
				end
			end
			function updateAmmo(itemKill,what)
				if what == "subtract" then
					local v68 = getLoader("v3item").inventory.get(itemKill);
					local v69 = v68 and v68.ammoManager;
					if v68 ~= nil and (v69 and (v69.ammo >= 1)) then
						local tt = v68 and v68.isConsumable
						if tt then
							v69:setAmmo(v69.ammo - 1);
						else
							v69:setAmmo((v69.ammo - v68 and v68.numProjectiles) or 1);    
						end
					end
				end
			end

							getgenv().selectedFoodfunc = selectedFood or 'Bandage' or "Cookie";
							local inventory =getLoader('v3item').inventory
							local oldItem = inventory.getEquippedItem();
							local healingItem = inventory.getFromName(selectedFoodfunc)
							local spawnProtected =  playerCharacter:FindFirstChild("ForceField")
							local isKnocked =  getLoader('ClientReplicator').Get(lp,'knocked')
							if isKnocked ~= true and playerHumanoid and playerHumanoid.Health > 0 then

								if (healingItem == nil) and getTotalSlotsUsed() < 32 then
									buyItem(selectedFoodfunc);
								end

								local itemData = getLoader('v3items').items[healingItem and healingItem.name]
								local v68 = healingItem and healingItem.ammoManager

								if selectedFoodfunc ~= 'Medkit' and ammoData ~= nil and (v68 ~= nil and v68.ammo ~= nil and v68.ammo <= ammoData.ammo - 1) then
									for i = 1, 3 do
										buyAmmo(selectedFoodfunc);
									end
								end							

								if not spawnProtected and isKnocked ~= true then
									if healingItem ~= nil and playerHumanoid.Health < playerHumanoid.MaxHealth and isautoheal ~= true then
										getgenv().isautoheal = true
										equip(healingItem.guid);
										useConsumable(healingItem.guid);
										updateAmmo(healingItem.guid,"subtract")
										equip(oldItem and oldItem.guid);
										local Ammo = getAmmo(healingItem);
										if (Ammo and (Ammo.ammo == 0)) then
											removeItem(healingItem.guid);
										end
										getgenv().isautoheal = false
									end
								end

							end
						end)()
						RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
					end
				end
			end}));

			function SetEquipped(item,b)
				local inventory = getLoader('v3item').inventory
				inventory.unequipAll()
				for l,v in next,getLoader('v3item').inventory.items do
					if v.name == item and v.SetEquipped then
						v:SetEquipped(b)
					end
				end
			end
