									v.Disabled = false;
								end
							end
							IsInvisible = true;
						else
							local StoredCF = FakeCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame;
							FakeCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = RealCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame;
							RealCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = StoredCF;
							FakeCharacter.Humanoid:UnequipTools();
							Player.Character = RealCharacter;
							workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = RealCharacter.Humanoid;
							PseudoAnchor = FakeCharacter.HumanoidRootPart;
							for i, v in pairs(FakeCharacter:GetChildren()) do
								if v:IsA("LocalScript") then
									v.Disabled = true;
								end
							end
							IsInvisible = false;
						end
					end
					MobileButtonNew()
					loadU:CreateConnection("InvisibleUserInputConnection", UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(key, gamep)
						if gamep then
							return;
						end
						if ((key.KeyCode.Name:lower() == Keybind:lower()) and CanInvis and RealCharacter and FakeCharacter) then
							if (RealCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and FakeCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
								Invisible();
							end
						end
					end));
				end
			end}));
		end)

            function setMinigunSpin(bool)
                if lp:GetAttribute('isMinigunSpinning') ~= bool then
                    lp:SetAttribute('isMinigunSpinning',bool)
                    getLoader('Signal').FireServer('setMinigunSpin',bool)
                end
            end

			function gunAttack(v3item, itemKill, v,id, guid4, typekill)
				if itemKill ~= nil and itemKill.name ~= 'Minigun' then
					equip(itemKill.guid);
					local eee = v3item.inventory
					local v68 = itemKill
					local v69 = v68 and v68.ammoManager;
					local itemData = eee.getEquippedItem();
					if itemData and itemData.name == itemKill.name then
						local gunModel = itemData.model;
						if (gunModel and gunModel.PrimaryPart and gunModel.PrimaryPart:FindFirstChild("Muzzle")) then
							local bulletCFrame = calculateReplicationCFrame(v.Position, itemData, gunModel);
							if v69 and v69.ammo and (v69.ammo > 0) then
								FireServer('replicateShot')
								v3item.projectiles.newProjectileOfType("bullet", {
									itemName = itemData.name,
									cframe = bulletCFrame,
									visualCFrame = bulletCFrame,
									guid = guid4,
									isPlayerOwned = true,
									length = itemData.projectileLength or 12,
									lifetime = itemData.projectileLifetime or 500,
									owner = lp
								});
								FireServer("replicateProjectiles", unpack({
									[1] = itemKill.guid,
									[2] = {
										[1] = {
											[1] = guid4,
											[2] = bulletCFrame
										}
									},
									[3] = itemData.firemode
								}));
								FireServer("projectileHit", unpack({
									[1] = guid4,
									[2] = typekill,
									[3] = {
										hitSize = v.Size,
										hitPart = v,
										pos = bulletCFrame,
										guid = typekill == 'nextbot' and id or nil,
										bot = typekill == 'nextbot' and v.Parent or nil,
										hitPlayerId = typekill == 'player' and id or nil
									}
								}));
								if (v69 and v69.ammo and (v69.ammo >= 1)) then
									v69:setAmmo((v69.ammo - v68.numProjectiles) or 1);
								end
							end
						end
					end
                elseif itemKill ~= nil and itemKill.name == 'Minigun' then
					equip(itemKill.guid);
					local eee = v3item.inventory
					local v68 = itemKill
					local v69 = v68 and v68.ammoManager;
					local itemData = eee.getEquippedItem();
					if itemData and itemData.name == itemKill.name then
						local gunModel = itemData.model;
						if (gunModel and gunModel.PrimaryPart and gunModel.PrimaryPart:FindFirstChild("Muzzle")) then
							local bulletCFrame = calculateReplicationCFrame(v.Position, itemData, gunModel);
							if v69 and v69.ammo and (v69.ammo > 0) then
                                setMinigunSpin(true)
								FireServer('replicateShot')
								v3item.projectiles.newProjectileOfType("bullet", {
									itemName = itemData.name,
									cframe = bulletCFrame,
									visualCFrame = bulletCFrame,
									guid = guid4,
									isPlayerOwned = true,
									length = itemData.projectileLength or 12,
									lifetime = itemData.projectileLifetime or 500,
									owner = lp
								});
								FireServer("replicateProjectiles", unpack({
									[1] = itemKill.guid,
									[2] = {
										[1] = {
											[1] = guid4,
											[2] = bulletCFrame
										}
									},
									[3] = itemData.firemode
								}));
								FireServer("projectileHit", unpack({
									[1] = guid4,
									[2] = typekill,
									[3] = {
										hitSize = v.Size,
										hitPart = v,
										pos = bulletCFrame,
										guid = typekill == 'nextbot' and id or nil,
										bot = typekill == 'nextbot' and v.Parent or nil,
										hitPlayerId = typekill == 'player' and id or nil
									}
								}));
								if (v69 and v69.ammo and (v69.ammo >= 1)) then
									v69:setAmmo((v69.ammo - v68.numProjectiles) or 1);
								end
                            elseif v69.ammo and v69.ammo == 0 then
                                setMinigunSpin(false)
							end
						end
                    else
                        setMinigunSpin(false)
					end
				end
			end

			function doGunStuff(v3item,equipped,item,clientrep,itemData,ammo,itemKill,gun)
				if not itemKill and getTotalSlotsUsed() < 32 then
					buyItem(gun);
				end
				if ammo ~= nil and ((ammo.ammoOut ~= nil) and (ammo.ammoOut < 30)) then
					for i = 1, 7 do
						buyAmmo(gun);
					end
				end
				if clientrep.Get(lp,'reloading') ~= true and itemData and itemData.data and ammo ~= nil and ((ammo.ammo <= itemData.data.ammo - 1)) then
					reload(clientrep,v3item,item,equipped);
				end		
			end			

			function isMoving(hum)
				local forcefield = hum.Parent and hum.Parent:FindFirstChild('ForceField')
				if hum and hum.Health > 0 and forcefield then
					if hum.MoveDirection.Magnitude > 0 then
						return true
					end
				end
				return false
			end

			function canAttackPlayer(plr)
				local chr = plr and plr.Character
				local forcefield = chr and chr:FindFirstChild('ForceField')
				local hum = chr and chr:FindFirstChild('Humanoid')
				local shouldAttack = forcefield and isMoving(hum) or not forcefield
				if plr and chr and hum and shouldAttack then
					return true
				end
				return false
			end


			local plrInteract={
				['gun kill'] = function(plr,old,loader)
					local guid4 = loader("GUID")();
					local v3item = loader('v3item')
					local clientrep = loader('ClientReplicator')
					local inventory = v3item.inventory
					local equipped = inventory.getEquippedItem()
					local getitem = inventory.getFromName(selectedallplrsinglemodeGun); 
					local itemData = loader('v3items').items[getitem and getitem.name]
					local v68 = getitem and getitem.ammoManager
					local itemKill= getitem and getitem.guid
					doGunStuff(v3item,equipped,getitem,clientrep,itemData,v68,itemKill,selectedallplrsinglemodeGun)
					local plrFoundThink = plr
					local v = players:FindFirstChild(plrFoundThink);
					local chr = v and v.Character
					local humanoid = chr and chr:FindFirstChild('Humanoid')
					local isKillable = canAttackPlayer(v) --not isMoving(humanoid) --chr and chr:FindFirstChild('ForceField') or not isMoving(humanoid)
					local head = chr and chr:FindFirstChild('Head')
					local root = chr and chr:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')
					local health = humanoid and humanoid.Health or 0 
					if v ~= nil and (chr and humanoid and head and root and isKillable) and health > 0 then
						gunAttack(v3item,getitem,head,v.UserId, guid4,'player');
					end	
				end,
				['blade kill'] = function(plr,old,loader)
					if players:FindFirstChild(plr) then
						local plrFound = players[plr];
						local plrFoundCall,_;
						if ((bankFarming ~= true) and plrFound and (isKillingPlayer ~= true) and plrFound.Character and
							plrFound.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and (plrFound.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0) and
							plrFound.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and canAttackPlayer(plrFound)) then
							local targetSelected = plrFound;
							local targetCharacter = targetSelected.Character;
							local targetPart = targetCharacter.HumanoidRootPart;
							local targetHumanoid = targetCharacter.Humanoid;
							while selectedplrsmode == 'blade kill' and selectedplr == plr and PlayerActionToggled and plrFoundCall ~= false and targetCharacter and canAttackPlayer(plrFound) and targetPart and targetHumanoid and targetHumanoid.Health > 0 do
								getgenv().isKillingPlayer = true;
								plrFoundCall, _ = pcall(function()
									-- workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = targetHumanoid;
									task.spawn(function()
										CFrameTP(plrFound.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * selectedplrposfunc())
									end);
									bladeKillPlr(plrFound);
								end);
								task.wait()
							end
							equip()
							if playerHumanoidRootPart then
								playerHumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
								playerHumanoidRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
								task.wait(0.1);
								CFrameTP(old);
								task.wait(0.2);
							end
							getgenv().isKillingPlayer = false;
							if plrFoundCall == false then
								v084('warn')(plrFoundCall,_)
							end

						end
					end		
				end,
				['auto teleport'] = function(plr,old,loader)
					if  players:FindFirstChild(plr) then
						local plrFound = players[plr];
						local plrFoundCall,_;
						if bankFarming ~= true and plrFound and plrFound.Character and plrFound.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and plrFound.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
							local targetSelected = plrFound;
							local targetCharacter = targetSelected.Character;
							local targetPart = targetCharacter.HumanoidRootPart;
							local targetHumanoid = targetCharacter.Humanoid;							
							while selectedplrsmode == 'auto teleport' and  selectedplr == plr and PlayerActionToggled and plrFoundCall ~= false and targetCharacter and targetPart do
								task.wait();
								getgenv().isTeleportingPlayer = true;
								plrFoundCall, _ = pcall(function()
									CFrameTP(plrFound.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * selectedplrposfunc());
								end);
							end
							getgenv().isTeleportingPlayer = false;
							if playerHumanoidRootPart then
								playerHumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
								playerHumanoidRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
								task.wait(0.1);
								CFrameTP(old);
								task.wait(0.2);
							end
							if plrFoundCall == false then
								v084('warn')(plrFoundCall,_)
							end
						end
					end
				end,
				['kill'] = function(plr,old,loader)
					if players:FindFirstChild(plr) then
						local plrFound = players[plr];
						local plrFoundCall;
						if ((bankFarming ~= true) and plrFound and plrFound.Character and
							plrFound.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and (plrFound.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0) and
							plrFound.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and canAttackPlayer(plrFound)) then
							local targetSelected = plrFound;
							local targetCharacter = targetSelected.Character;
							local targetPart = targetCharacter.HumanoidRootPart;
							local targetHumanoid = targetCharacter.Humanoid;
							local LAST_KNOCK_TIME = 0;
							local KNOCK_COOLDOWN = 2.5;
							while selectedplrsmode == 'kill' and selectedplr == plr and PlayerActionToggled and plrFoundCall ~= false and targetCharacter and canAttackPlayer(plrFound) and targetPart and targetHumanoid and targetHumanoid.Health > 0 do
								task.wait();
								getgenv().isKillingPlayer = true;
								plrFoundCall, _ = pcall(function()
									if (selectedplrpos == "custom") then
										workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = targetHumanoid;
										equip(getItemGUID(false, "Fists"));
										-- unbindCameraEquipped()
										CFrameTP(plrFound.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame *
													selectedplrposfunc(plrcf1 or 0, plrcf2 or 0, plrcf3 or 0));
										knockPlr(plrFound);
										stompPlr(plrFound);
									else
										workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = targetHumanoid;
										equip(getItemGUID(false, "Fists"));
										-- unbindCameraEquipped()
										CFrameTP(plrFound.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * selectedplrposfunc());
										knockPlr(plrFound);
										stompPlr(plrFound);
									end
								end);
							end
							workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = playerHumanoid;
							equip()
							if playerHumanoidRootPart then
								playerHumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
								playerHumanoidRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
								task.wait(0.1);
								CFrameTP(old);
								task.wait(0.2);
							end
							getgenv().isKillingPlayer = false;
						end
					end					
				end,
				['spectate'] = function(plr)
					if players:FindFirstChild(plr) then
						local xcallo,opp;
						local x09 = players[plr]
						local pchr = x09 and x09.Character
						local humanoid = pchr and pchr:FindFirstChild('Humanoid')
						if humanoid then
							while selectedplrsmode == 'spectate' and selectedplr == plr and PlayerActionToggled and xcallo ~= false and humanoid.Parent ~= nil do
								xcallo,opp = pcall(function()
									workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = humanoid;	
								end)						
								task.wait(0.3)
							end
							workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = playerHumanoid
						end
					end					
				end
			}
			indexUIObj("players", "autoteleport", z001.players:Toggle({
				Title = selectedplrsmode or WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get("plrsMode", true) or "auto teleport",
				Value = false,
				Type = "Toggle",
				Callback = function(h)
					getgenv().PlayerActionToggled = h;
					if (selectedplr ~= nil) then
						while PlayerActionToggled == true do
							local plrModeNow = selectedplrsmode
							local old = playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame
							local loader= getLoader
							if plrInteract[plrModeNow] then
								plrInteract[plrModeNow](selectedplr,old,loader)

							end
							RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
						end
					end
				end
			}))

			if selectedallplrsinglemodeGun == nil then
				local v0 = WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get("selectedGunSingle", true) or 'AK-47'
				getgenv().selectedallplrsinglemodeGun = v0 
			end

			if z001.players.autoteleport ~= nil then
				z001.players.autoteleport:SetTitle(selectedplrsmode)
			end


			z001.players:Space()

			indexUIObj("players", "playersattackOptionMain", z001.players:Dropdown({Title="",Values={"fists","guns","blades"},Value=(WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get("playersAttack4", true) or "fists"),Callback=function(h)
				if (z001.players.playersattackOption ~= nil) then
					WindUI.saveDataSettings:LoadDataIf("playersAttack4", h);
				end
				getgenv().mainSelectedAllPlayerMode = h;
				if h== 'guns' then
					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.autokillall,false)
					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersattackOption,false)
					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersfistsattackdis,false)

					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.autokillallblades,false)


					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.autokillallguns,true)
					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersattackGun,true)
					if selectedallplrmodeGunAt == 'nearest' then
						hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersgunattackdis,true)
					else
						hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersgunattackdis,false)
					end
					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersattackOptionGun,true)
				elseif h == 'fists' then
					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.autokillallguns,false)
					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersattackGun,false)
					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersgunattackdis,false)
					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersattackOptionGun,false) 

					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.autokillallblades,false)


					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.autokillall,true)
					hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersattackOption,true)
					if h == 'fists' and selectedallplrmode == 'nearest' then
						hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersfistsattackdis,true)
					elseif h =='fists' and selectedallplrmode ~= 'nearest' then
						hideObject(z001.players and z001.players.playersfistsattackdis,false)

			--[[]]

			function makeFOVCircle(v_1,v_C,v_T)
				local v_1func = fovVisible or v_1 or false
				getgenv().ffovcircle = Drawing.new("Circle")
				ffovcircle.Visible = v_1func
				ffovcircle.Radius = fovSize or 20
				ffovcircle.Color = v_C 
				ffovcircle.Thickness = v_T
				ffovcircle.Filled = false
				ffovcircle.Position = Vector2.new(camera.ViewportSize.X / 2,camera.ViewportSize.Y / 2 )
			end
			function getfovsize()
				if fovSize ~= nil then
					ffovcircle.Radius = fovSize
				end
			end
		end)

					if humanoid and target and humanoid.Parent == target.Parent then

						end
					end
				end

		function replicateEffects(typev, pos,equipped)
			local loader = getLoader
			local clientrep = loader('ClientReplicator')
			local reloading =clientrep.Get(lp, "reloading")
			if reloading ~= true and equipped then
				loader("v3effect").ReplicateEffect(typev, {position=pos});
			end
		end
		getgenv().magickSpammer = {
			RPG = {
				count = 0,
				lastFireTime = 0,
				fireCooldown = 00.9, -- Your original cooldown
				projectileFired = false,
				activeProjectileGuid = nil,
				maxHits = 20, -- Your original hit limit
				hitDelay = 0.09 -- Faster hits than my previous version
			}
		}
		function rpgHit(args,v3item)
			local t = args
			local inventory = v3item.inventory
			local equipped = inventory.getEquippedItem()
			local Signal = getLoader('Signal')
			if equipped and equipped.name == 'RPG' and magickSpammer.RPG.projectileFired then
				Signal.FireServer('rocketHit', unpack(args))
				magickSpammer.RPG.count = magickSpammer.RPG.count + 1
				
				if magickSpammer.RPG.count >= magickSpammer.RPG.maxHits then
					magickSpammer.RPG.projectileFired = false
					magickSpammer.RPG.count = 0
					magickSpammer.RPG.activeProjectileGuid = nil
				end
			end
		end

		function replicateProjectiles(args)
			local Signal = getLoader('Signal')
			Signal.FireServer('replicateProjectiles', unpack(args))
		end

		function fireProjectile(equipped, targetChar,guid)
			local currentTime = tick()
			if currentTime - magickSpammer.RPG.lastFireTime >= magickSpammer.RPG.fireCooldown then
				magickSpammer.RPG.lastFireTime = currentTime
				magickSpammer.RPG.projectileFired = true
				magickSpammer.RPG.count = 0
				
				local projectileGuid = guid()
				magickSpammer.RPG.activeProjectileGuid = projectileGuid
				
				replicateProjectiles({
					[1] = equipped.guid,
					[2] = {
						[1] = {
							[1] = projectileGuid,
							[2] = targetChar
						}
					},
					[3] = "semi"
				})
				
				return projectileGuid
			end
			return nil
		end
		function manageAmmo(clientrep,v3item,equipped)
			local v68 = equipped and equipped.ammoManager
			if v68 ~= nil then
				if (v68.ammoOut ~= nil) and (v68.ammoOut < 2) then
					for i = 1, 4 do
						buyAmmo(equipped.name)
					end
				end
				
				if magickSpammer.RPG.projectileFired then
					if clientrep.Get(lp,'reloading') ~= true and v68.ammo ~= nil and v68.ammo == 0 then
						reload(clientrep,v3item,equipped,equipped)
					elseif v68 and v68.ammo and v68.ammo >= 1 then
						v68:setAmmo((v68.ammo - (equipped.numProjectiles or 1)))
					end
				end
			end
		end

		function noDelayProximity()
			for i,v in next,workspace:GetDescendants() do
				if v:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
					v["HoldDuration"] = 0
				end
			end
			loadU:CreateConnection('noDelayProximity',ProximityPromptService.PromptButtonHoldBegan:Connect(function(v)
				v["HoldDuration"] = 0
			end))
		end

		function getNextBots()
			local w = {}
			local e = workspace:WaitForChild('NextBots')
			if e then
				for l,v in next,e:GetChildren() do
					table.insert(w,v)
				end
			end
			return w
		end

		-- Helper function to handle the attack logic
		function attackTarget(v3item,equipped, targetPart,guid)
			if not magickSpammer.RPG.projectileFired then
				fireProjectile(equipped, targetPart.CFrame,guid)
			end
			if magickSpammer.RPG.projectileFired then
				getgenv().ispam = true
				replicateEffects('baserocketexplosion', targetPart.Position, equipped)
				rpgHit({
					[1] = magickSpammer.RPG.activeProjectileGuid or guid(),
					[2] = guid(),
					[3] = targetPart.Position,
				},v3item)
				task.wait(magickSpammer.RPG.hitDelay)
			end
		end

		function getFarmerPosition()
			if farmerPos == 'hidden' then
				return CFrame.new(0,-4.9,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90),0,0)
			else
				return CFrame.new()
			end
		end

					table.insert(cache, v);
				end
			end
			return cache;
		end

		local HPOT = {}

		waitForPrimaryPart = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(instance, timeout)
			if instance:IsA('Model') and instance.ClassName ~= 'MeshPart' then
				timeout = timeout or 5 -- 5 second default timeout
				local start = tick()
				
				while not instance.PrimaryPart and (tick() - start) < timeout do
					task.wait(0.3)
				end
			end
			return instance.PrimaryPart ~= nil
		end)

		function b094(instance, primaryPart,from)
            if instance:GetAttribute('blacklist') then
                return true
            end	             
			instance:SetAttribute('blacklist',true)
			local cframe = primaryPart.CFrame
			if not table.find(honeypotBlacklist, cframe) then
				table.insert(honeypotBlacklist, cframe)
			end    
			task.delay(2, function()
				if instance and instance.Parent then
					--instance:Destroy()
				end
			end)
			__loadNow.sendBypassLog({
				cframe = tostring(cframe),
				model = instance,
				Parent = instance.Parent,
				detectedFrom = from or 'failed to get caller'
			})
		end		
		
		
		function findTrans(ins)
			if not ins then return nil end -- Add nil check for safety
			
			if ins:IsA("TouchTransmitter") then
				return ins,ins.Parent
			end
			
			if typeof(ins) == "Instance" then
				for _, child in ipairs(ins:GetChildren()) do
					local result = findTrans(child)
					if result then
						return result,result.Parent
					end
				end
			end
			
			return nil -- Explicit return for clarity
		end

        b0987 = function(instance)
            if instance:GetAttribute('blacklist') then
                return true
            end	  
            local part = instance.PrimaryPart
            if instance and part and instance:GetAttribute('isReady') ~= true then
                for _, avoidCFrame in pairs(honeypotBlacklist) do
                    local distance = (avoidCFrame.Position - part.Position).Magnitude
                    
                    if part.CFrame == avoidCFrame then
                        if LRM_ScriptVersion == nil then
                            v084('warn')('CAUGHT BY EXACT CFrame MATCH')
                        end
                        b094(instance, part, 'b0987')
                        return true
                    end
                    
                    if distance < 30 then
                        if LRM_ScriptVersion == nil then

                            v084('warn')('CAUGHT BY POSITION PROXIMITY',part.Position,'[avoidcframe] '..tostring(avoidCFrame))
                        end
                        b094(instance, part, 'b0987')
                        return true
                    end
                end
                return false
            end
            return false
        end
		function b0989(atm)
            if atm:GetAttribute('blacklist') then
                if LRM_ScriptVersion == nil then						
					local IntValue =  atm:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("IntValue")
					local str = IntValue and IntValue.Value or 'NOT BUNDLE'
                    v084('print')(atm,'is blacklisted returning true',str)

                end
                return true
            end	            
			if not atm or not atm:IsA("Instance") then
                if LRM_ScriptVersion == nil then
                    v084('print')(atm,'is nil or not available returning false')

                end
				return false
			end
			if not atm:IsA('Model') then
				if LRM_ScriptVersion == nil then

					v084('print')(atm,'is a model returning false')

				end
				return false
			end				
			local itemName = atm:GetAttribute('itemName')			
			local shouldCheck = itemName ~= 'Treasure Map'	and itemName ~= 'Tomahawk'	and itemName ~= 'Ninja Star'	
			if atm.ClassName ~= 'MeshPart' and shouldCheck then
                
				if b0987(atm) then
                    if LRM_ScriptVersion == nil then
						local IntValue =  atm:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("IntValue")
						local str = IntValue and IntValue.Value or 'NOT BUNDLE'
                        v084('print')(atm,'caught by another function returning true',str)
                    end

					return true
				end							
			
				local primaryPart = atm.PrimaryPart
				if not primaryPart then
                    if LRM_ScriptVersion == nil then

                        v084('print')(atm,'no primarypart returning false')
                    end
					return false
				end							
				local nearbyParts = workspace:GetPartsInPart(primaryPart)
				for _, part in ipairs(nearbyParts) do
					if part.Name == "Terrain Rocks" and part:IsA("Part") then
						local distance = (primaryPart.Position - part.Position).Magnitude
						local maxDistance = math.max(part.Size.X, part.Size.Y, part.Size.Z) / 2 + 5						
						if distance < maxDistance then
							b094(atm, primaryPart,'b0989')
                            if LRM_ScriptVersion == nil then
								local IntValue =  atm:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("IntValue")
								local str = IntValue and IntValue.Value or 'NOT BUNDLE'
                                v084('warn')(atm,'is honeypotted by main function',atm.Name,tostring(atm.Parent),str)
                            end
							return true
						end
					end
				end   
				local p,tt = findTrans(atm)
				if p and tt then
					for e,r in next,tt:GetTouchingParts() do
						if r.Name == "Terrain Rocks" then
							b094(atm, primaryPart,'b0989')
                            if LRM_ScriptVersion == nil then
								local IntValue =  atm:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("IntValue")
								local str = IntValue and IntValue.Value or 'NOT BUNDLE'
                                v084('warn')(atm,'is honeypotted by backup function gtps',atm.Name,tostring(atm.Parent),str)
                            end
							return true
						end						
					end
				end					             
			end			
			return false
		end

		function HPOT.SetListeners(id,pathName)
			local path = typeof(pathName) == 'Instance' and pathName
			loadU:CreateConnection(id,path.ChildAdded:Connect(function(...)
				local r, t = ...
				task.spawn(function()
					if r.ClassName ~= 'MeshPart' and r:IsA('Model') and waitForPrimaryPart(r) then
						local w = b0989(r)
						if w == false then
							r:SetAttribute('isReady',true)
						end
					end					
				end)
			end))
			local e = workspace:FindFirstChild('Game')
			if e then
				for i, v in pairs(path:GetChildren()) do
					task.spawn(function()
						if v.ClassName ~= 'MeshPart' and waitForPrimaryPart(v) then
							local w = b0989(v)
							if w == false then
								v:SetAttribute('isReady',true)
							end						
						end						
					end)
				end
			end			
		end

		function HPOT.IsInstanceReadyForFarm(...)
			local i = ...
			return i:GetAttribute('isReady')
		end


		HPOT.SetListeners('ATM_WATCH',workspace.ATMs)

		function getatms()
			for _, v in next, workspace.ATMs:GetChildren() do 
				local isready = HPOT.IsInstanceReadyForFarm(v) or v:GetAttribute('isReady') 
				local part = v.PrimaryPart
				local health = v:GetAttribute('health')
				local isDestroyed = v:GetAttribute('isDestroyed') 				
				if part and isready and not isDestroyed and health > 0 and not table.find(atmsCache,v) then
					table.insert(atmsCache,v)
				end
			end
			return atmsCache
		end

		function getcashregisters(b)
			local _o = {}
			if b == true then

				for l,v in next,workspace.Game.Props.CashRegister:GetChildren() do
					local state = v:GetAttribute('state')
					local health = v:GetAttribute('health')
					if state ~= 'destroyed' and health ~= 0 then					
						table.insert(_o,v)
					end
				end
			end
			return _o
		end

		function isnotalreadyfarming()
			return (seasonalFarming ~= true and JewelryFarm.State.IsFarming ~= true and JewelryFarm.State.IsBreakingRubble ~= true and getgenv().checkedAIMKILLING ~= true and getgenv().slotFarming ~= true and getgenv().farmingFurnitureCases~= true and getgenv().PirateShipFarming~= true and getgenv().truckFarming ~= true and getgenv().isAirdropThrowing ~= true and getgenv().spectralScytheFarming ~= true and JewelryFarm.IsFarming ~= true and JewelryFarm.IsBreakingRubble ~= true and  getgenv().farmingPrinter ~= true and getgenv().airDropFarming ~= true and getgenv().rockFarming ~= true and getgenv().destroyingBankDoor ~= true and getgenv().isFarmingVehicle ~= true and getgenv().treasureFarming ~= true and getgenv().rareGemsFarming ~= true and getgenv().cashFarming ~= true and getgenv().bankFarming~= true and getgenv().isFarmingSafe~= true and IsItemFarmerActive()~= true  and getgenv().isOpeningArmory~= true and getgenv().atmFarming ~= true)
		end

			if (z001.cash.atmfarm ~= nil) then

			end
			getgenv().atmFarm = h;
			if atmFarming == true and atmFarm == false then
				getgenv().atmFarming = false
			end
			if getgenv().atmFarm == true then
                while getgenv().atmFarm == true and not adminDetected do 
                    task.wait(.6)
                    if isnotalreadyfarming() then

                    local inventory = getLoader('v3item').inventory
                    local equipped = inventory.getEquippedItem()
                    local fists = inventory.getFromName('Fists')				
                    local old = playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        local atms = getatms()
						local numatms = #atms
                        local registers = getcashregisters(numatms == 0)
                        if numatms > 0 then
                            local atmindex = math.random(1,#atms)
                            local atm = atms[atmindex]
                            local isReady = atm:GetAttribute('isReady')
                            local atmId = atm:GetAttribute('atmId')
                            local health = atm:GetAttribute('health')
                            local isDestroyed = atm:GetAttribute('isDestroyed')             
                            local isFarmerActive = IsItemFarmerActive()	
                            if playerHumanoidRootPart and isnotalreadyfarming() and isFarmerActive == false and bankFarming ~= true and destroyingBankDoor ~= true and airDropFarming ~= true and playerHumanoidRootPart and atm and atm.PrimaryPart and health > 0 and atmFarming ~= true and not atm:GetAttribute('BeingFarmed') and isReady then
                                local success, errorMsg
                                atm:SetAttribute('BeingFarmed', true)									
                                -- loopTP(atmFarm,atm:GetAttribute('BeingFarmed') ~= false,atm.PrimaryPart)
                                while not adminDetected and playerHumanoidRootPart and not destroyingBankDoor and atmFarm and success ~= false and atm and atm.PrimaryPart and atm:GetAttribute('BeingFarmed') ~= false do task.wait(.002)
                                    success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                                        if atm ~= nil and atm.Parent and atm.PrimaryPart  then
											atm.PrimaryPart.Transparency = 0.8
											atm.PrimaryPart.Anchored = true
                                            getgenv().atmFarming = true
											local atmDmgThread 	
											local atmExitThread
                                            local health = atm:GetAttribute('health')
                                            local isDestroyed = atm:GetAttribute('isDestroyed')                
                                            local targetPosition = atm.PrimaryPart.Position
                                            local desiredCFrame = atm.PrimaryPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -1)
                                            local characterPosition = desiredCFrame.Position
                                            local distance = (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position - targetPosition).Magnitude
                                            -- playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame = farmerPos ~= 'hidden' and CFrame.lookAt(characterPosition, targetPosition) or atm.PrimaryPart.CFrame * getFarmerPosition()
											-- playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame = farmerPos ~= 'hidden' and atm.PrimaryPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,-1,0) or atm.PrimaryPart.CFrame * getFarmerPosition()										

											playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame = farmerPos ~= 'hidden' and atm.PrimaryPart.CFrame or atm.PrimaryPart.CFrame * getFarmerPosition()										
                                            local damageAmount = 8
                                            local newHealth = atmDMG == 'instant' and 0 or math.max(0, health - damageAmount)									
											if atmDmgThread == nil then
												atmDmgThread = task.delay(1, function()
													if atm and atm.Parent and atm.PrimaryPart then
														if health ~= 0 then
															atm:SetAttribute('health', newHealth)   
															atmDmgThread =nil
														end                    
													end
												end)		
											end							
                                            if health <= 0 or isDestroyed then
												if atmExitThread == nil then
													atmExitThread = task.delay(1.5, function()
														if atm and atm.Parent then
															atm:SetAttribute('BeingFarmed', false)
															-- atm:Destroy()	
															atmExitThread = nil											
														end
													end)
												end
                                            end
                                        end                
                                    end)
                                end
								if success == false then
									v084('ATMFARM',errorMsg)
								end
								checkforerror(success,v084('warn'), errorMsg,v084('getinfo')(2,'nl'));
                                --until atm:GetAttribute('BeingFarmed') == false or spectralScytheFarming or destroyingBankDoor == true or atmFarm == false or success == false or not atm or not atm.Parent or not atm.PrimaryPart --or isnotalreadyfarming() ~= true --or (bankFarming == true) or ((bankFarm == true) and (getBankCash() > 0)) or IsItemFarmerActive() == true
                                updateATMCount(atm)
                                cashpickup()
                                if atm and atm.Parent then
                                    atm:SetAttribute('BeingFarmed', false)
                                end
                                playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame = farmmodes == 'regular' and old or CFrame.new(1653.3216552734375, -16.953155517578125, -529.6856079101562);
                                task.wait()

                                SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)								
                                task.delay(farmingDelay,function()
                                    getgenv().atmFarming = false	

                                end)
                                if atmFarm == false then break end							
                            end
                        elseif #registers > 0 then
                            local xind = math.random(#registers)
                            local v = registers[xind]
                            local state = v:GetAttribute('state')
                            local health = v:GetAttribute('health')
                            if v.PrimaryPart and state ~= 'destroyed' and health ~= 0  and playerHumanoidRootPart then
                            	-- repeat task.wait()
								local exitThread
                                local success, errorMsg
                                while not adminDetected and playerHumanoid and playerHumanoid.Parent and atmFarm and success ~= false and v and v.PrimaryPart and v:GetAttribute('BeingFarmed') ~= false do task.wait(.002)
									success,errorMsg = pcall(function()
										v.PrimaryPart.Transparency = 0.8
										v.PrimaryPart.Anchored = true
										getgenv().atmFarming = true;
										state =v:GetAttribute('state')							
										health = v:GetAttribute('health')										
										local targetPosition = v.PrimaryPart.Position
										local desiredCFrame = v.PrimaryPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -1)
										local characterPosition = desiredCFrame.Position
										local distance = (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position - targetPosition).Magnitude
										--playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame = farmerPos ~= 'hidden' and CFrame.lookAt(characterPosition, targetPosition) or v.PrimaryPart.CFrame * getFarmerPosition()										
										playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame = farmerPos ~= 'hidden' and v.PrimaryPart.CFrame or v.PrimaryPart.CFrame * getFarmerPosition()										
										equip(fists and fists.guid);
										if fists and fists.equipped then
											FireServer("attackMeleeHit",unpack({[1]="prop",[2]={meleeType=punchmodes[math.random(#punchmodes)],guid=v:GetAttribute("guid")}}));
										end
										cashpickup();
										if health <= 0 or state == 'destroyed' then
											if exitThread == nil then
												exitThread = task.delay(.5, function()
													if v and v.Parent then
														v:SetAttribute('BeingFarmed', false)
														-- atm:Destroy()		
														exitThread = nil										
													end
												end)
											end
										end	
									end)
								end									
                            	--until v:GetAttribute('BeingFarmed') == false or atmFarm == false
								checkforerror(success,v084('warn'), errorMsg,v084('getinfo')(2,'nl'));
								
                            	CFrameTP(farmmodes == 'regular' and old or CFrame.new(1653.3216552734375, -16.953155517578125, -529.6856079101562))
                            	equip(equipped and equipped.guid)
                                if v and v.Parent then
                                    v:SetAttribute('BeingFarmed', false)
                                end								
                            	task.wait()
                            	SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)
                            	task.delay(farmingDelay,function()
                            		getgenv().atmFarming = false
                            	end)
                            end
                            
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
	
		end}));

		function getRocks()
			local rocks = {}
			for l,v in next,workspace.Rocks:GetChildren() do
				table.insert(rocks,v)
			end
			return rocks
		end

		findProximityPrompt = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(instance)
			if instance:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
				return instance
			end
			
			for _, child in pairs(instance:GetChildren()) do
				local result = findProximityPrompt(child)
				if result then
					return result
				end
			end
			
			return nil
		end)		

		findClickDetector = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(instance)
			if instance:IsA("ClickDetector") then
				return instance
			end
			
			for _, child in next,instance:GetChildren() do
				local result = findClickDetector(child)
				if result then
					return result
				end
			end
			
			return nil
		end)		

		function mineRock(rock)
			local w ,r = pcall(function()
				local hitbox =rock and rock:FindFirstChild('Hitbox')
				local prompt = hitbox and findProximityPrompt(hitbox) or hitbox:FindFirstChild('ProximityPrompt')

				local ss = prompt:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Enabled'):Connect(function()
					prompt.Enabled = true
				end)	
				local bb = prompt:GetPropertyChangedSignal('RequiresLineOfSight'):Connect(function()
					prompt.RequiresLineOfSight = false
				end)
				prompt.RequiresLineOfSight = false
				if prompt and replicatingMine ~= true then
					prompt.MaxActivationDistance = 35
					getgenv().replicatingMine = true
					prompt:InputHoldBegin()
					wait(prompt.HoldDuration)  -- Wait for hold duration
					prompt:InputHoldEnd()
					getgenv().replicatingMine = false
					ss:Disconnect()
					ss = nil
					bb:Disconnect()
					bb = nil													
				end
			end)   
		end

		function loopTeleport(i,inv)
			if not i and i.PrimaryPart then return end
			local e = i.PrimaryPart
			local w = inv.getFromName('Pickaxe')
			repeat task.wait()
				equip(w and w.guid)
				local targetPosition = e.Position
				local desiredCFrame = e.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -4.3)
				local characterPosition = desiredCFrame.Position        
				
				playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.lookAt(characterPosition, targetPosition)      
			until bankFarming == true or destroyingBankDoor or not e or e.Parent == nil or i:GetAttribute('numOres') == 0 or inv.getFromName('Pickaxe') == nil or rockFarm == false
		end

	
		indexUIObj("cash", "diamondore", z001.cash:Toggle({Title='ore farm',Value=WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get("diamondOreFarm"),Icon="check",Type="Toggle",isPaidFunction=true,Callback=function(h)
			if (z001.cash.diamondore ~= nil) then
				WindUI.saveDataSettings:LoadDataIf("diamondOreFarm", h);
			end
			getgenv().rockFarm = h
			if rockFarm == false and rockFarming == false then
				getgenv().rockFarming = false
			end
			while getgenv().rockFarm == true and not adminDetected do task.wait(1.3)

				local old= farmmodes == 'regular' and playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame or CFrame.new(1653.3216552734375, -16.953155517578125, -529.6856079101562);
				local inventory = getLoader('v3item').inventory
				local hasItem = inventory.getFromName('Pickaxe')
				local rocks = getRocks()
				if hasItem and #rocks>0 and playerHumanoidRootPart then
					equip(hasItem.guid)
					local rockindex = math.random(#rocks)
					local v = rocks[rockindex]
					local primarypart = v.PrimaryPart
					if isnotalreadyfarming() and primarypart and rockFarming ~= true then
						task.spawn(loopTeleport,v,inventory)
						repeat task.wait()
							getgenv().rockFarming = true
							if replicatingMine ~= true then
								task.delay(.8,mineRock,v)
							end
						until adminDetected or v:GetAttribute('numOres') == 0  or v.PrimaryPart == nil or v.PrimaryPart.Parent == nil or rockFarm == false or inventory.getFromName('Pickaxe') == nil
						CFrameTP(old)
						task.wait()

						SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)								
						task.delay(farmingDelay,function()
							getgenv().rockFarming = false						
						end)
						if rockFarm == false then 
							getgenv().replicatingMine = false 
							break
						end					
					end
				elseif not hasItem and getTotalSlotsUsed() < 32 then
					buyItem('Pickaxe')
				end
			end

		end}));	
					
		function extractNumber(moneyString)
			local cleanedString = string.gsub(moneyString, '[$,]', '')
			local numberValue = tonumber(cleanedString)
			
			return numberValue
		end


		function getBankCash()
			local bankCash = workspace.BankRobbery:FindFirstChild("BankCash");
			local xcashp =lp:GetAttribute('bankCash')
			if xcashp then	
				return xcashp
			else
				return 0
			end
		end
		function SetFarmSpecial(vvd)
			getgenv().itemspecialfarm = vvd;
		end

		function delCashIf(timer,v)
			if timer < 1 then
				v:Destroy()
			end
		end

		HPOT.SetListeners('CASH_WATCH',workspace.Game.Entities.CashBundle)
		HPOT.SetListeners('LunarNewYear',workspace.LunarNewYear)


		function GetCash()
			local cache = {}
			local e = workspace:FindFirstChild('Game')
			if not e then return end
			local Entities = e:FindFirstChild('Entities')
			local CashBundle = Entities:FindFirstChild('CashBundle')
			if CashBundle then
				for i,v in next,CashBundle:GetChildren() do
					if not v:GetAttribute('blacklist') and v:IsA("Model") and v:GetAttribute('isReady') == true then
						table.insert(cache,v)
					end
				end
			end
			return cache
		end
		function getOthers(type)
			local c = {}
			local e = workspace:FindFirstChild('Game')
			if not e then return end
			local Other = e:FindFirstChild('Other')		
			if Other then	
				for l,v in next,Other:GetChildren() do 
					if v.Name == type then
						table.insert(c,v)
					end
				end
			end
			return c
		end

		function getVehicles()
			local w = {}
			local e = workspace:WaitForChild('Game')
			if e then
				local Vehicles = e:FindFirstChild('Vehicles')
				if Vehicles then
					for l,v in next,Vehicles:GetChildren() do
						table.insert(w,v)
					end
				end
			end
			return w
		end

		function getnum(t)
			if t ~= nil and typeof(t) == 'Instance' then
				return #t:GetChildren()
			elseif  t ~= nil and typeof(t) == 'table' then
				return #t
			end
		end

		function removeForceField()
			if playerCharacter and playerCharacter:FindFirstChild('ForceField') then
				local fists = getItemGUID(false,'Fists')
				equip(fists)
			end
		end

		function thrower(item,lastThrowTime,currentTime)
			local ammoManager = getAmmo(item)
			-- if ammoManager and ammoManager.ammo <= 1 then
			-- 	for i = 1,5 do buyAmmo('TNT')end											
			-- end				
			if item and not item.equipped then
				equip(item.guid)
			end
			if item and item.equipped then
				throwItem({[1]=item.guid,[2]=Vector3.new(0, 0, 0),[3]=Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)})
				ammoManager:setAmmo(ammoManager.ammo - 1)
				if ammoManager and ammoManager.ammo and ammoManager.ammo == 0 then
					removeItem(item.guid)
				end				
			end
		end				
		indexUIObj("cash", "truckfarm", z001.cash:Toggle({Title='truck farm',Value=WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get("truckFarm"),Icon="check",Type="Toggle",isPaidFunction=true,Callback=function(h)
			if (z001.cash.truckfarm ~= nil) then
				WindUI.saveDataSettings:LoadDataIf("truckFarm", h);
			end
			getgenv().truckFarm = h
			local alreadFound = false
			if truckFarm == false and truckFarming then
				getgenv().truckFarming = false
				alreadFound = false
			end
			while getgenv().truckFarm == true and not adminDetected do 
				task.wait(0.5)
				local old= farmmodes == 'regular' and playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame or CFrame.new(1653.3216552734375, -16.953155517578125, -529.6856079101562);
				if alreadFound ~= true and isnotalreadyfarming() and playerHumanoidRootPart then
					local vehicles = getVehicles()
					if alreadFound ~= true then
						for l,v in next,vehicles do
							
							if isnotalreadyfarming() and v.PrimaryPart and v.Name == 'Armored Truck' then
								local trucky = v:GetAttribute('blacklist') ~= true and v
								local truckCash = trucky and trucky:FindFirstChild('TruckCash')
								if trucky and truckCash and truckCash.PrimaryPart then
									local cash = truckCash:FindFirstChild('Cash')
									local main = truckCash and truckCash:FindFirstChild('Main')
									if cash and main and getnum(cash) > 0 then
										alreadFound = true
										local m,k
										repeat task.wait()
											m,k = pcall(function()
												local CFramew = truckCash.PrimaryPart.CFrame or main.CFrame or main.WorldPivot
												getgenv().truckFarming = true
												cash = truckCash:FindFirstChild('Cash')
												local prox = findProximityPrompt(truckCash)
												CFrameTP(CFramew * CFrame.new(0, -2.7, -1) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0))
												fireproximityprompt(prox)	
											end)								
										until adminDetected or m == false or cash == nil or getnum(cash) == 0 or v.Parent == nil or v.PrimaryPart == nil or v.PrimaryPart.Parent == nil or truckFarm == false
										checkforerror(m,v084('warn'), k,v084('getinfo')(2,'nl'));
										CFrameTP(old)
										task.wait()
										SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)
										task.delay(farmingDelay,function()
											getgenv().truckFarming = false
										end)								
									end
								else
									if not v:GetAttribute('blacklist') then
										trucky:SetAttribute('blacklist',true)
									end
								end
							end
						end
					end				
					local events = getOthers("Event Armored Truck")
					if getTotalSlotsUsed() < 32 and #events > 0 and isnotalreadyfarming() and alreadFound ~= true then
						alreadFound = true
						local load= getLoader
						local v3item = load('v3item')
						local inventory = v3item.inventory
						local tnt = inventory.getFromName('TNT')
						if tnt == nil then
							buyItem('TNT')
							buyAmmo('TNT')
							tnt = inventory.getFromName('TNT')								
						end					
						if tnt then
							local truck = events[1]
							local part = truck.PrimaryPart
							if isnotalreadyfarming() and truck and part then
								local lastThrowTime = 0            
								repeat task.wait()
									getgenv().truckFarming = true
									CFrameTP(truck and truck.PrimaryPart and truck.PrimaryPart.CFrame)
									task.spawn(function()
										local currentTime = os.time()
										if currentTime - lastThrowTime >= 3 then
											local tnt = inventory.getFromName('TNT')
											local ammoManager = getAmmo(tnt)

											if tnt == nil then
												buyItem('TNT')
												task.wait(.2)
												for i = 1,5 do buyAmmo('TNT')end
												tnt = inventory.getFromName('TNT')								
											end
											if tnt then
												if ammoManager and ammoManager.ammo and ammoManager.ammo <= 1 then
													local needed = 5 - ammoManager.ammo
													for i = 1,needed do buyAmmo('TNT')end											
												end												
												equip(tnt.guid)
												local equipped = tnt.equipped
												if equipped then
													for i = 1,ammoManager.ammo do
														thrower(tnt)												
													end
													lastThrowTime = currentTime
												end
											end
										end
									end)
								until adminDetected or #getOthers("Event Armored Truck") == 0 or #events == 0 or truck.PrimaryPart == nil or truck.PrimaryPart.Parent == nil or truck.Parent == nil or getgenv().truckFarm == false
								CFrameTP(old)
								task.wait()
								SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)
								task.delay(farmingDelay,function()
									getgenv().truckFarming = false
								end)
							end
						end
						alreadFound = false					
					end
				end
			end
		end}));

									getgenv().airDropFarming = true
									part = v and v.PrimaryPart
									prximity = part and part:FindFirstChild('ProximityPrompt')
									CFrameTP(part.CFrame)
									if prximity ~= nil then
										fireproximityprompt(prximity)
									end
									if whe >= 170 then
										v:Destroy()
									end
								end)
							until adminDetected or airdrop == false or r == false or not v.PrimaryPart or v.Parent == nil or prximity.Enabled == false or v.PrimaryPart:FindFirstChild('ProximityPrompt').Enabled==false 
							checkforerror(r,v084('warn'), t,v084('getinfo')(2,'nl'));

							playerHumanoidRootPart.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.new()
							playerHumanoidRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new()
							CFrameTP(old)
							task.wait()

							SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)								
							if part ~=nil then
								part.AssemblyLinearVelocity=Vector3.new(99999999,10000000000,0)
							end
							task.delay(farmingDelay,function()
								getgenv().airDropFarming = false
                                part.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)							
							end)
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end}));

			if (z001.cash.cashfarm ~= nil) then

			end
			getgenv().CashFarm = h
			if CashFarm == false and cashFarming == true then
				getgenv().cashFarming = false
			end

				if isnotalreadyfarming() then

				local oldpos = farmmodes == 'regular' and playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame or CFrame.new(1653.3216552734375, -16.953155517578125, -529.6856079101562);

							local cashtime = 50

									end
									--cashpickup()

								end)
                            end
							checkforerror(e,v084('warn'),f,v084('getinfo')(2,'nl'));

							--until isReady ~= true or isFarmingSafe == true or CashFarm == false or not v.PrimaryPart or e == false --or bankFarm == true and getBankCash() > 0 or atmFarm and atmFarming == true

				end
			end
		end}));

		function attackMob(...)
			task.wait(1.2)
			local inst = ...
			task.spawn(function()
				if mobFarm == true and inst and not b0987(inst) then
					local health
					repeat task.wait(.4)
						health = inst:GetAttribute('health')
						task.delay(.4,function()
							if health ~= 0 then

								local damageAmount = 10
								local newHealth = math.max(0, health - damageAmount)								
								inst:SetAttribute('health',newHealth)	
							end
						end)
					until health == 0 or mobFarm == false
				end				
			end)
		end	
		waitForClickDetector = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(instance, timeout)
			if instance.ClassName == 'MeshPart' then
				timeout = timeout or 5 -- 5 second default timeout
				local start = tick()
				
				while not instance:FindFirstChildOfClass('ClickDetector') and (tick() - start) < timeout do
					task.wait(0.3)
				end
			end
			return instance:FindFirstChildOfClass('ClickDetector')
		end)
		function collectCandy(...)
			task.wait(.3)
			local inst = ...
			if inst.ClassName == 'MeshPart' then
				local d = waitForClickDetector(inst,10) --inst:FindFirstChildOfClass('ClickDetector')
				if d ~= nil then
					task.delay(.1,function()						
						fireclickdetector(d)
					end)
				end
			end
		end		
		local hlwList = CreateIf(function()		
			local christms = workspace:FindFirstChild('Christmas')
			if christms and christms:FindFirstChild('Elf') and christms.Elf:FindFirstChild('Hitbox') then
				local po = findProximityPrompt(christms.Elf.Hitbox)
				if po then
					fireproximityprompt(po)
				end

				loadU:CreateConnection('ElfListener',christms.Elf.Hitbox.ChildAdded:Connect(function(...)
					local inst = ...
					local po = findProximityPrompt(inst)
					if po then
						fireproximityprompt(po)
					end

				end))				
			end
			if christms and christms:FindFirstChild('Mobs') then			
				loadU:CreateConnection('MobListener',christms.Mobs.ChildAdded:Connect(attackMob))
			end
		end)

		if hlwList then
			hlwList()
		end

		getAllSafes = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			local specialSafes = {};
			local e = workspace:FindFirstChild('Game')
			if e then
				local schest = workspace.Game.Entities.SmallChest:GetChildren();
				local ss = workspace.Game.Entities.SmallSafe:GetChildren();
				local ms = workspace.Game.Entities.MediumSafe:GetChildren();
				local ls = workspace.Game.Entities.LargeSafe:GetChildren();
				local lchest = workspace.Game.Entities.LargeChest:GetChildren();
				local js = workspace.Game.Entities.JewelSafe:GetChildren();
				local gs = workspace.Game.Entities.GoldJewelSafe:GetChildren();
				if (#schest > 0) then
					for i, v in next,schest do
						if (v:GetAttribute("isOpen") ~= true) then--and not b0987(v) then
							table.insert(specialSafes, v);
						end
					end
				end
				if (#lchest > 0) then
					for i, v in next,lchest do
						if (v:GetAttribute("isOpen") ~= true) then -- and not b0987(v) then
							table.insert(specialSafes, v);
						end
					end
				end
				if (#ss > 0) then
					for i, v in next,ss do
						if (v:GetAttribute("isOpen") ~= true) then --and not b0987(v) then
							table.insert(specialSafes, v);
						end
					end
				end
				if (#ms > 0) then
					for i, v in next,ms do
						if (v:GetAttribute("isOpen") ~= true) then -- and not b0987(v) then
							table.insert(specialSafes, v);
						end
					end
				end
				if (#ls > 0) then
					for i, v in next,ls do
						if (v:GetAttribute("isOpen") ~= true) then --and not b0987(v) then
							table.insert(specialSafes, v);
						end
					end
				end
				if (#js > 0) then
					for i, v in next,js do
						if (v:GetAttribute("isOpen") ~= true) then --and not b0987(v) then
							table.insert(specialSafes, v);
						end
					end
				end
				if (#gs > 0) then
					for i, v in next,gs do
						if (v:GetAttribute("isOpen") ~= true) then --and not b0987(v) then
							table.insert(specialSafes, v);
						end
					end
				end
				if ((#specialSafes > 0) and safeFarm) then
					getgenv().foundSafes = true;
				else
					getgenv().foundSafes = false;
				end
			end
			return specialSafes;
		end)
		getBankDoorPosition = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(bank)
			local bankrobbery = bank or workspace.BankRobbery
			local place = bankrobbery and bankrobbery:FindFirstChild('VaultDoor')
			local dse = place and place:FindFirstChild('Door')
			if dse then
				return dse.Position
			end
		end)
		distanceSafe = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(v)
			local pos = getBankDoorPosition();
			if v.ClassName ~= 'MeshPart' and (pos and v.PrimaryPart) then
				return (pos - v.PrimaryPart.Position).magnitude , v.PrimaryPart;
			end
		end)		

		function destroyBankDoor(old,bool,oldItem)
			local bankrobbery = workspace.BankRobbery
			local place = bankrobbery and bankrobbery:FindFirstChild('VaultDoor')	
			local door = place and place:FindFirstChild('Door')
			if bankrobbery and place and bool and door and destroyingBankDoor ~= true then
				local p0 = os.time()
				local lastThrowTime = 0			
				local p,o 
				while not adminDetected and p ~= false and bankrobbery:FindFirstChild('VaultDoor') and bool do
					p,o = pcall(function()
						getgenv().destroyingBankDoor = true
						CFrameTP(door.CFrame)
						local currentTime = os.time()
						if currentTime - lastThrowTime >= 5.5 then
							buyItem("TNT")
							buyAmmo('TNT')
							local inventory = getLoader('v3item').inventory
							local tnt = inventory.getFromName('TNT')
							if not tnt then
								buyItem('TNT')
								buyAmmo('TNT')
							end
							if tnt then
								equip(tnt.guid)
							end
							thrower(tnt,lastThrowTime,currentTime)
							lastThrowTime = currentTime
						end						
					end)
					task.wait()
				end
				checkforerror(p,v084('warn'),o,v084('getinfo')(2,'nl'));
				local hh,yy = pcall(function()
					CFrameTP(CFrame.new(1124.21533, 8.21989441, -348.212921, -0.99305141, 1.0139277e-08, 0.117681503, 3.12030646e-09, 1, -5.98280323e-08, -0.117681503, -5.90451066e-08, -0.99305141))
					playerHumanoid.Jump = true
					task.wait(.1)
					SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)
					CFrameTP(workspace.BankRobbery.BankAlarmTrigger.CFrame)
					task.wait(.3)

					if workspace.BankRobbery.AlarmLights.Rotation == Vector3.new(0, -90, 0) then
						playerHumanoid.Jump = true

						CFrameTP(workspace.BankRobbery.BankAlarmTrigger.CFrame)
						playerHumanoid.Jump = true

						CFrameTP(CFrame.new(1120.99561, 8.21989441, -337.819855, -0.981598735, 4.57376146e-08, 0.19095543, 6.27914147e-08, 1, 8.32569143e-08, -0.19095543, 9.37152436e-08, -0.981598735))
						if playerHumanoid and playerHumanoidRootPart then
							playerHumanoid:MoveTo(Vector3.new(playerHumanoidRootPart.Position.X,playerHumanoidRootPart.Position.Y,playerHumanoidRootPart.Position.Z + 10))
						end
						SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)
					end
				end)	
				if not hh then
					v084('warn')(hh,yy)
				end

				task.wait(.85)
				equip(oldItem and oldItem.guid)						
				CFrameTP(old)	
				task.wait()
				SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)
				task.delay(farmingDelay,function()
					getgenv().destroyingBankDoor= false						
				end)							
			end
		end
		checkBankDoor = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(itempart,olds,boov,oldItem)
			if getTotalSlotsUsed() < 32 then
				local bankrobbery = workspace.BankRobbery
				local place = bankrobbery and bankrobbery:FindFirstChild('VaultDoor')
				local door = place and place:FindFirstChild('Door')
				if destroyingBankDoor ~= true and boov == true and place and door and itempart ~= nil then
					local distance = (door.Position - itempart.Position).Magnitude
					local p0 = os.time()
					local lastThrowTime = 0
					local t,e;
					if distance <= 65 then
						repeat 
							task.wait()
							t,e = pcall(function()

								if door then
									getgenv().destroyingBankDoor = true
									CFrameTP(door.CFrame)
									local currentTime = os.time()
									if currentTime - lastThrowTime >= 5.5 then
										buyItem("TNT")
										buyAmmo('TNT')
										local inventory = getLoader('v3item').inventory
										local tnt = inventory.getFromName('TNT')
										if not tnt then
											buyItem('TNT')
											buyAmmo('TNT')
										end
										if tnt then
											equip(tnt.guid)
										end
										thrower(tnt,lastThrowTime,currentTime)
										lastThrowTime = currentTime

									end								
								end
							end)
						until adminDetected or t == false or boov == false or not bankrobbery or not bankrobbery:FindFirstChild('VaultDoor') or not bankrobbery.VaultDoor:FindFirstChild('Door')
						checkforerror(t,v084('warn'),e,v084('getinfo')(2,'nl'));
						
						local hh,yy = pcall(function()
							CFrameTP(CFrame.new(1124.21533, 8.21989441, -348.212921, -0.99305141, 1.0139277e-08, 0.117681503, 3.12030646e-09, 1, -5.98280323e-08, -0.117681503, -5.90451066e-08, -0.99305141))
							task.wait(.2)
							SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)
							CFrameTP(CFrame.new(1124.70081, 8.21989441, -343.19223, -0.999578297, 1.84696241e-08, -0.0290373806, 1.55443942e-08, 1, 1.00965842e-07, 0.0290373806, 1.00471901e-07, -0.999578297))
							CFrameTP(CFrame.new(1120.99561, 8.21989441, -337.819855, -0.981598735, 4.57376146e-08, 0.19095543, 6.27914147e-08, 1, 8.32569143e-08, -0.19095543, 9.37152436e-08, -0.981598735))
							if playerHumanoid and playerHumanoidRootPart then
								playerHumanoid:MoveTo(Vector3.new(playerHumanoidRootPart.Position.X,playerHumanoidRootPart.Position.Y,playerHumanoidRootPart.Position.Z + 10))
							end
							SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)
						end)

						if not hh then
							v084('warn')(hh,yy)
						end

						task.wait(.85)
						equip(oldItem and oldItem.guid)						
						CFrameTP(olds)	
						task.wait()
						SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)
						task.delay(farmingDelay,function()
							getgenv().destroyingBankDoor= false						
						end)				
					end
				end
			end
		end)		
		checkIfSafesLocked = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			if atmFarming then return end
			local allSafes = getAllSafes();
			for l, v in next, allSafes do
				local distance,part = distanceSafe(v);
				local plrpos = part ~= nil and (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position - part.Position).Magnitude
				if ((distance ~= nil) and (distance <= 65)) then 
					if workspace.BankRobbery:FindFirstChild('VaultDoor') then 
						return true
					end
				end
			end
			return false
		end)			
		local blentities = {}
		function checkIfItemIsBankLocked(item)
			local bankRobbery = workspace:FindFirstChild('BankRobbery')
			local trigger = bankRobbery:FindFirstChild('BankAlarmTrigger')
			if not bankRobbery then
				return false
			end
			if not bankRobbery:FindFirstChild('VaultDoor') then
				return false
			end
			if blentities[item] then
				return true
			end
			local extraSize = Vector3.new(5, 0, 1)
			local rootPart = item:FindFirstChild("Root") or item:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
			if rootPart then
				local relativePos = trigger.CFrame:PointToObjectSpace(rootPart.Position)
				local halfSize = (trigger.Size / 2) + extraSize
				
				if math.abs(relativePos.X) <= halfSize.X and math.abs(relativePos.Y) <= halfSize.Y and math.abs(relativePos.Z) <= halfSize.Z and not blentities[item] then
					--item:SetAttribute('bankLocked',true)
					blentities[item] = true
					return true
				end
			end
			return false
		end

		function openNearestSafe()
			task.spawn(function()
				buyItem('Lockpick')
				local d = getAllSafes()
				for l,v in next,d do
					local p = v.PrimaryPart
					local prox = findProximityPrompt(v)
					if p then
						local distance = (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position-p.Position).Magnitude
						if distance <= 45 and prox then
							fireproximityprompt(prox)
						end
					end
				end
			end)
		end

			if (z001.cash.bankfarm ~= nil) then

			if bankFarming == true and bankFarm == false then
				getgenv().bankFarming = false
			end
			while getgenv().bankFarm == true and not adminDetected do
                
				getgenv().atmfarmmode = farmmodes or "regular";
				local oldIr = getLoader('v3item').inventory.getEquippedItem()
				local oldc = atmfarmmode ~= 'afk' and playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame or CFrame.new(1653.3216552734375, -16.953155517578125, -529.6856079101562);
				local b0 = getBankCash();

				local mainCFrame = bankCash and bankCash:FindFirstChild('Main') 
				local cashv =  workspace:FindFirstChild('BankRobbery') and workspace.BankRobbery:FindFirstChild('BankCash')
				if isnotalreadyfarming() and bankRobbery and bankCash and (b0 > 0) and bankFarming ~= true and playerHumanoidRootPart then
					local hh,yy;
                    while not adminDetected and hh ~= false and bankFarm and b0> 0 and playerCharacter and playerHumanoidRootPart and playerHumanoid and playerHumanoid.Health > 1 do

								if bankRobbery:FindFirstChild('VaultDoor') then
									destroyBankDoor(oldc,bankFarm,oldIr)
								else										
									getgenv().bankFarming = true; -- -2.7
									CFrameTP(mainCFrame.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -3, -1) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0));
									if b0 > 0 then
										task.spawn(function()
											local pr = findProximityPrompt(bankCash)
											if pr then
												fireproximityprompt(pr)
											end												
										end)
									end											
								end							
							end							
						end)
                        task.wait()                        
                    end
					checkforerror(hh,v084('warn'),yy,v084('getinfo')(2,'nl'));
					
					if hh == false then
						v084('warn')('BANKFARM',yy)
					end
					equip(oldIr and oldIr.guid)
					CFrameTP(oldc);
					task.wait()
					SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)								
					task.delay(farmingDelay,function()
						getgenv().p09e = false
						getgenv().bankFarming = false;					
					end)
				end	
				task.wait(0.1);
			end					
		end}));
		getTreasure = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			local tresleft = {}
			local treasure = workspace.Game.Local.Debris
			for i,k in pairs(treasure:GetChildren()) do
				if k.Name == "TreasureMarker" then
					table.insert(tresleft,k)
				end
			end
			return tresleft
		end)
		indexUIObj("cash", "treasureFarm", z001.cash:Toggle({Title=tcmod == nil and "treasure farm" or tcmod == 'chinese' and '宝藏农场',Value=WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get("treasureFarm"),Icon="check",Type="Toggle",isPaidFunction=true,Callback=function(h)
			if (z001.cash.treasureFarm ~= nil) then
				WindUI.saveDataSettings:LoadDataIf("treasureFarm", h);
			end
			if treasureFarm == false and treasureFarming then
				getgenv().treasureFarming=false
			end
			getgenv().treasureFarm = h;

							while not adminDetected and ci ~= false and  prox do task.wait()
								ci,cc = pcall(function()
									getgenv().treasureFarming = true
									CFrameTP(k.CFrame)
								
									if prox then
										fireproximityprompt(prox)
										cashpickup()
									end
									prox = findProximityPrompt(k)
								end)
							end
							checkforerror(ci,v084('warn'),cc,v084('getinfo')(2,'nl'));
							
							equip(oldi and oldi.guid)
							CFrameTP(oldpos)
							task.wait()

							SetHumanoidEnabled(lp,true)

								getgenv().treasureFarming = false
							end)

					end
				end
			end
		end}));
		function validateFarmReady()
			local isAtmFarmReady = (atmFarming ~= true)
			return isAtmFarmReady and (bankFarm ~= true or (bankFarm == true and getBankCash() == 0))
		end

		function throwItem(v)
			FireServer("throwItem", unpack(v));
		end

		function JewelryFarm:GetTargetJewelry()
			return self.Settings.JewelryType == "all" and self.Jewelry.All or self.Jewelry.Rare
		end

		function JewelryFarm:GetJewelryLocation()
			if not workspace:FindFirstChild("GemRobbery") then return nil end
			return workspace.GemRobbery
		end

		function JewelryFarm:GetRubble()
			local location = self:GetJewelryLocation()
			if not location or not location:FindFirstChild("Rubble") then return {} end
			return location.Rubble:GetChildren()
		end

		function JewelryFarm:GetCases(yieldType)
			local location = self:GetJewelryLocation()
			if not location or not location:FindFirstChild("JewelryCases") then return {} end
			
			local cases = {}
			local caseFolder = location.JewelryCases:FindFirstChild(yieldType .. "YieldSpawns")
			if caseFolder then
				for _, case in pairs(caseFolder:GetChildren()) do
					table.insert(cases, case)
				end
			end
			return cases
		end

		function JewelryFarm:GetHighYieldCases()
			return self:GetCases("High")
		end

		function JewelryFarm:GetLowYieldCases()
			return self:GetCases("Low")
		end

		function JewelryFarm:CountAvailableJewelry(cases, jewelryList)
			local available = {}
			for _, case in pairs(cases) do
				for _, jewelName in pairs(jewelryList) do
					if case:FindFirstChild(jewelName) and not table.find(available,case) then
						table.insert(available, case)
					end
				end
			end
			return available
		end

		function JewelryFarm:ShouldFarm()
			return isnotalreadyfarming()
		end

		function JewelryFarm:Cleanup()
			self.State.IsFarming = false
			self.State.IsBreakingRubble = false
			self.State.Attempts = 0
		end

		function throw()
			local v3item = getLoader('v3item')	
			local inventory = v3item.inventory
			local itemdata = inventory.getFromName('TNT')
			local item = itemdata and itemdata.guid
			if itemdata == nil then
				buyItem("TNT")
				buyAmmo('TNT')	
				-- itemdata = inventory.getFromName('TNT')		
				-- item = itemdata and itemdata.guid
				throw()
				--call function 
			end
			equip(item)
			task.wait(.1)
			local equipped = inventory.getEquippedItem()

			if equipped and equipped.guid == item then
				-- 'checked')
				task.delay(.3,function()
					throwItem({[1]=item,[2]=Vector3.new(0, 0, 0),[3]=Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)})
					task.wait()
					throwItem({[1]=item,[2]=Vector3.new(0, 0, 0),[3]=Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)})
					task.wait(.2)
					removeItem(item)

				end)
            else
                throw()
			end	
		end

		function JewelryFarm:BreakRubble(oldCFrame)
            local rubble = self:GetRubble()            
			if  #rubble == 0 or (tick() - self.State.LastRubbleBreak) < 5.8  then
                -- if #rubble == 0 and self.State.IsBreakingRubble== true then
    			-- 	self.State.IsBreakingRubble = false
                -- end

				return false
			end

			-- "Breaking rubble...")
			self.State.IsBreakingRubble = true

			-- Hold position in separate thread
			local startTime = tick()
			task.spawn(function()
				while not adminDetected and #rubble > 0 and (tick() - startTime) < 5.7 and self.Settings.Enabled and not destroyingBankDoor do
					CFrameTP((function()
                        if (tick() - startTime) < 2 then
                            return workspace.ItemsOnSale["Bundle of TNT"].TouchDetector.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 15, 0)
                        else
                            return CFrame.new(1653.3216552734375, -16.953155517578125, -529.6856079101562)

                        end
                    end)())
					task.wait()
				end
                CFrameTP(oldCFrame)
			end)

			-- Immediately buy and throw TNT while position is held
			if self.Settings.Enabled then
                -- 'attemptingThrow')
				throw()
			end
			
			self.State.LastRubbleBreak = tick()

            -- task.delay(farmingDelay,function()
            --     if #self:GetRubble() == 0 then
            --         JewelryFarm.State.IsBreakingRubble = false
            --     end
            -- end)    
            if not self.State.LoopWaiting then
                self.State.LoopWaiting = true
                while not adminDetected and #self:GetRubble() > 0 and (tick() - startTime) < 6.5 do task.wait()
                    local availableHighJewelry = self:CountAvailableJewelry(self:GetHighYieldCases(), self.Jewelry.All)
                    if #availableHighJewelry > 0 then
                        -- "High yield jewelry available - destroying rubble and farming now!")

                        if #self:GetRubble() > 0 then
                            rubble[1].Parent:Destroy()
                        end
                    end                    
                    -- 'waiting') 
                end
                self.State.IsBreakingRubble = false
                self.State.LoopWaiting = nil
                
            end
			return true
		end


        workspace.GemRobbery.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(...)
            local v,c = ...
            if v.Name == 'Rubble' and JewelryFarm.State.IsBreakingRubble then
                JewelryFarm.State.IsBreakingRubble = false
            end
        end)        

		function JewelryFarm:FarmCases(cases, oldCFrame)
			local targetJewelry = self:GetTargetJewelry()
			
			for _, case in pairs(cases) do
				for _, jewelName in pairs(targetJewelry) do
					if not self.Settings.Enabled then--or not self:ShouldFarm() then
						return
					end
					
					local jewel = case:FindFirstChild(jewelName)
					if jewel then
						local prompt = jewel:FindFirstChild("ProximityPrompt", true)
						
						if prompt then
							
							while self.Settings.Enabled and case:FindFirstChild(jewelName) and jewel:FindFirstChild("ProximityPrompt", true) and not destroyingBankDoor do --and self:ShouldFarm() do
    							self.State.IsFarming = true
								removeForceField()

								openNearestSafe()
								CFrameTP(jewel.WorldPivot * CFrame.new(0, -1.6, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0))
								
								if case:FindFirstChild('Glass') and case.Glass.Transparency ~= 1 then
									equip(getItemGUID(false, "Fists"))
									meleeItemHit({[1]="jewelcase",[2]={meleeType="meleepunch",guid=case:GetAttribute("guid")}})
								end
								
								fireproximityprompt(prompt)
								task.wait()
							end
							task.delay(farmingDelay,function()
								self.State.IsFarming = false
								
							end)
						end
					end
				end
			end
			
			CFrameTP(oldCFrame)
		end



		function JewelryFarm:Start(oldCFrame)
			if self.Settings.Enabled then return end
			
			self.Settings.Enabled = true
			self:Cleanup()
			
			task.spawn(function()
				while not adminDetected and self.Settings.Enabled do task.wait(0.2)
					if not self:ShouldFarm() then
						task.wait(1)
					else
						local rubble = self:GetRubble()
						local highYieldCases = self:GetHighYieldCases()
						local lowYieldCases = self:GetLowYieldCases()
						
						-- STEP 1: Always check rubble first
						if #rubble > 0 then
							-- "Rubble detected - breaking rubble first")
							self:BreakRubble(oldCFrame)
							
							-- Immediately check for high yield jewelry - if it spawned, destroy rubble
							local availableHighJewelry = self:CountAvailableJewelry(highYieldCases, self.Jewelry.All)
							if #availableHighJewelry > 0 then
								-- "High yield jewelry available - destroying rubble and farming now!")

								if #rubble > 0 and rubble[1] and rubble[1].Parent then
									rubble[1].Parent:Destroy()
								end
								self:FarmCases(highYieldCases, oldCFrame)
							end
						else
							-- STEP 2: No rubble - farm high yield jewelry
							local availableHighJewelry = self:CountAvailableJewelry(highYieldCases, self:GetTargetJewelry())
							if #availableHighJewelry > 0 then
								-- "Farming high yield jewelry")
								self:FarmCases(highYieldCases, oldCFrame)
							else
								-- STEP 3: No high yield - farm low yield jewelry
								local availableLowJewelry = self:CountAvailableJewelry(lowYieldCases, self:GetTargetJewelry())
								if #availableLowJewelry > 0 then

									-- "Farming low yield jewelry")
									self:FarmCases(lowYieldCases, oldCFrame)
								else
									-- "No jewelry available - waiting...")
									task.wait(2)
								end
							end
						end
					end
				end
				
				self:Cleanup()
			end)
		end


		function JewelryFarm:Stop()
			self.Settings.Enabled = false
			self:Cleanup()
		end

		function JewelryFarm:Toggle()
			if self.Settings.Enabled then
				self:Stop()
			else
				self:Start()
			end
		end

		getAllEntity = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			local cache = {};
			local e = workspace:FindFirstChild('Game')
			if e then
				for i, v in pairs(workspace.Game.Entities.CashBundle:GetChildren()) do
					table.insert(cache, v);
				end
				for i, v in pairs(workspace.Game.Entities.ItemPickup:GetChildren()) do
					table.insert(cache, v);
				end
			end
			return cache;
		end)
		getNearestStuff = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(inventory)
			local entities = getAllEntity();
			for l, v in next, entities do
				if v.ClassName ~= 'MeshPart' and v.PrimaryPart then
					local itemname = v:GetAttribute('itemName')
					local itemCheck = itemname == 'Military Armory Keycard' and inventory.getFromName(itemname) == nil or true					
					local dis = (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position - v.PrimaryPart.Position).magnitude;
					if ((not table.find({'Component Box'},itemname)) and (dis <= 9) and v:GetAttribute("isNew")) and itemCheck then
						return v;
					end
				end
			end
		end)
		doExtra = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(inventory)
			local nearestStuff = getNearestStuff(inventory);

				CFrameTP(nearestStuff.PrimaryPart.CFrame);
				Collect(nearestStuff);
			end
		end)

			end
			return 0;
		end

		end
