		function claimCraft()
			if getLoader('Signal').InvokeServer ~= nil then
				local sdd = (lp:GetAttribute("craftCompletionTime")
					or 0) <= getLoader("GetLocalUTCTime")() 
				if sdd then
					InvokeServer("claimCraft")
					getgenv().craftingStill = false
				end
			end
		end

		function getCrafts()
			local caxhe = {}
			local l_load_0 = getLoader
			if l_load_0('crafts').recipes ~= nil then
				for l,c in next,l_load_0("crafts").recipes do
					table.insert(caxhe,l)
					table.sort(caxhe)
				end
			else
				caxhe = {
					"-"
				}
			end
			return caxhe
		end
		hasComp = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(v22)
			for v23, v24 in next,v22 do
				local v25 = "component_" .. v23;
				if (lp:GetAttribute(v25) or 0) < v24 then
					return false;
				end;
			end;
			return true;
		end)

		refrehTime = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(v78,v75)
			if v78 and v75 then 
				return getLoader("secondsToClock")(v78 - v75) 
			end 
		end)
		
		
		getTime = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(vq)
			local l_load_0 = getLoader
			if craftingStill and vq and checkIngred(vq) then
				local v75 = l_load_0("GetLocalUTCTime");
				local v42 = lp:GetAttribute("craftCompletionTime") or 0;
				if v42 and v75 then
					local cft = l_load_0("crafts").recipes[vq]
					if z001 and z001.cash and z001.cash.autocrafter ~= nil then
						local lof = tcmod == nil and 'crafting: ' or tcmod == 'chinese' and '制作中: '
						local transtime = tcmod == nil and 'time left: ' or tcmod == 'chinese' and '剩余时间: '
						z001.cash.autocrafter:SetDesc(lof..string.lower(vq).."\n"..transtime..refrehTime(v42,v75()))
					end
				end
			elseif craftingStill and vq and not checkIngred(vq) then
				local v75 = l_load_0("GetLocalUTCTime");
				local v42 = lp:GetAttribute("craftCompletionTime") or 0;
				local cft = l_load_0("crafts").recipes[vq]
				if v42 and v75 and z001 and z001.cash and z001.cash.autocrafter ~= nil then
					local lof = tcmod == nil and 'crafting: ' or tcmod == 'chinese' and '制作中: '
					local translatedcraftalert = tcmod == nil and "alert: no components for next " or tcmod == 'chinese' and '警告: 没有足够的材料制作下 '
					local transtime = tcmod == nil and 'time left: ' or tcmod == 'chinese' and '剩余时间: '
					z001.cash.autocrafter:SetDesc(lof..string.lower(vq).."\n"..transtime..refrehTime(v42,v75()).."\n"..translatedcraftalert..string.lower(ItemCFunc))
				end
			end
		end)

		checkIngred = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(ItemCFuncer)
			local itemcraft = getLoader("crafts").recipes and getLoader("crafts").recipes[ItemCFuncer]
			if not itemcraft then
				return 
			else
				local ingr = itemcraft.ingredients
				ingrcheck = function(ingr)
					if ingr.items then
						iv1 = ingr.items and getLoader("v3item").inventory.hasItems(ingr.items)
					end
				end
				ingrcheck2 = function(ingr)
					if ingr.components then
						iv2 = ingr.components and hasComp(ingr.components)
					end
				end
				ingrcheck(ingr)
				ingrcheck2(ingr)
				if not ingr.items then
					iv1 = true
				end
				if not ingr.components then
					iv2 = true
				end
				return iv1 and iv2
			end
		end)
		function doAutoCraft(vw)
			local loader = getLoader('Signal')
			local getluct = getLoader("GetLocalUTCTime");
			local atrib1 = lp:GetAttribute("currentCraft") 
			local atrib2 = lp:GetAttribute("currentCraftClaimed")
			local v41 = atrib1 and not atrib2
			local v42 = lp:GetAttribute("craftCompletionTime") or 0;
			if atrib1 then
				getgenv().craftingStill = true
			end
			if vw and atrib1 ~= vw and checkIngred(vw) then
				if autoCrafter == true then
					getgenv().craftingStill = true
					InvokeServer("beginCraft",vw)
				end
			elseif lp:GetAttribute("currentCraft") and (lp:GetAttribute("craftCompletionTime") or 0) <= getluct() and getTotalSlotsUsed() < 32 then
				InvokeServer("claimCraft")
				getgenv().craftingStill = false
				return true
			end
		end
		spawn(function()
			local ff = workspace:FindFirstChild("Fireworks")
			if ff then
				for l,v in next,ff:GetChildren() do
					v:SetAttribute('health',0)
				end
			end
		end)

		_stepAutoCraftTime = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			if z001 and z001.cash and z001.cash.autocrafter ~= nil then
				if autoCrafter and ItemCFunc and checkIngred(ItemCFunc) then
					getgenv().debounceCraft = false
					getTime(ItemCFunc)
				elseif autoCrafter and ItemCFunc and not checkIngred(ItemCFunc) and not craftingStill then
					z001.cash.autocrafter:SetDesc("alert: missing components for "..string.lower(ItemCFunc))
				elseif autoCrafter and checkIngred(ItemCFunc) and craftingStill then
					getTime(ItemCFunc)
				elseif autoCrafter == false and ItemCFunc and doAutoCraft(ItemCFunc) ~= true and craftingStill then
					getTime(ItemCFunc)
				elseif autoCrafter and ItemCFunc and doAutoCraft(ItemCFunc) and not craftingStill then
					z001.cash.autocrafter:SetDesc("waiting for next craft...")
				elseif autoCrafter and not doAutoCraft(ItemCFunc) and not checkIngred(ItemCFunc) and craftingStill then
					getTime(ItemCFunc)
				end
			end
		end)

		loadU:CreateConnection('autoCraftDescUpdater',RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(_stepAutoCraftTime))

		end

		getAllReward = function()
			local load= getLoader 
			local lpp= load('GuiLoader')
			local rewardtable={}
			if lpp and lpp.Get ~= nil then
				for l,v in next,lpp.Get('PlaytimeRewards').Frame.Pages.Rewards.Today.Rewards:GetChildren() do 
					if v.Name ~= 'UIGridLayout' then
						table.insert(rewardtable,v)
					end
				end
				for l,v in next,lpp.Get('PlaytimeRewards').Frame.Pages.DailyRewards.Rewards:GetChildren() do 
					if string.find(v.Name,'Daily') then
						local claim = v:FindFirstChild('Claim')
						if claim ~= nil and claim:FindFirstChild('Holder') and claim.Holder:FindFirstChild('Button') then
							if string.find(claim.Holder.Button.Text,'CLAIM') then
								table.insert(rewardtable,v)
							end
						end
					end
				end
			end
			return rewardtable
		end


		function DestroyNearestATM()
			local models = getatms()
			local v3item = getLoader('v3item')
			local inventory= v3item.inventory

			local equipped = inventory.getEquippedItem()
			for i,k in pairs(models) do
				if equipped and equipped.name == 'Fists' then
					if playerHumanoidRootPart then
						local mp = k.PrimaryPart

						if mp then
							local distance = (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position - mp.Position).magnitude
							local health =k:GetAttribute("health") 
							if health > 0 and distance <= 35 then
								k:SetAttribute('health',0)
								cashpickup()
							end
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end

		function checkitems()
			local inventory = getLoader('v3item').inventory
			for l,v in next,inventory.currentItemsData do
				for o,p in ipairs(gemthings()) do
					if not v.isStashed and v.name == p then
						return v.guid
					end
				end
			end
			return nil
		end

		function checkGemCases(str)
			local available = 0
			if str and str:FindFirstChild('Furniture') then
				for l,v in next,str.Furniture:GetChildren() do
					local furnitureName = v:GetAttribute('furnitureName')
					local count,isNotFull = v55(v)
					if furnitureName == 'LongGemDisplay' and count ~= 3 then
						available = available + 1
					elseif (furnitureName == "GemDisplay2" or furnitureName == "FloatingGemDisplay") and count ~= 1 then
						available = available + 1
					elseif (furnitureName == 'LuxuryGemCabinet' or furnitureName == 'GemCabinet') and count ~= 12 then
						available = available + 1
					end
				end
			end
			return available
		end

		function isGemHolder(inst)

		function sellItem(item)
			local f = getLoader('v3item').inventory.get(item)
			local sellPrice = validateSell(item)
			if tetraxData.dealerData.isDealerCooldown ~= true and sellPrice <= tetraxData.dealerData.cash  then
				FireServer("sellItem", item);
			end
		end

		function setDealerCooldownTimer()
			local formatnumb = getLoader("commavalue")
			if tetraxData.dealerData.remainingCooldownSeconds <= 0 and tetraxData.dealerData.sec ~= nil then
				resetDealer()
				loadU:CleanConnection('dealerCooldown') 
			end
			if z001 and z001.cash and z001.cash.autoSell ~= nil then
				if autoSell and z001.cash.autoSell ~= nil then
					if tetraxData.dealerData.cash <= 300 and tetraxData.dealerData.isDealerCooldown then
						z001.cash.autoSell:SetDesc('cash: $'..(tetraxData.dealerData.cash or 0)..'\nalert: dealer is low'..'\n'..'restock: '..getLoader('secondsToClock')(tetraxData.dealerData.remainingCooldownSeconds))
					elseif tetraxData.dealerData.remainingCooldownSeconds ~= 0 then
						z001.cash.autoSell:SetDesc('restock: '..tostring(getLoader('secondsToClock')(tetraxData.dealerData.remainingCooldownSeconds)))
					end
				elseif autoSell == false and z001.cash.autoSell ~= nil then
					z001.cash.autoSell:SetDesc(nil)
				end
			end
		end

		function autoDeleteOnce(timer,v)
			if autoDestroyLocked == true and timer <= .7 then
				v:Destroy()
			end
		end
		function Collect(s)
			task.spawn(function()
				local Click = findClickDetector(s)
				if Click then
					fireclickdetector(Click)
				end								
			end)
		end		
		HPOT.SetListeners('ITEMS_WATCH',workspace.Game.Entities.ItemPickup)
		GetItems = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
			local cache = {};
			local e= workspace:FindFirstChild('Game')
			if not e then return end
			local Entities = e:FindFirstChild('Entities')
			if Entities then
				local ItemPickup = Entities:FindFirstChild('ItemPickup')
				if ItemPickup then
					for i, v in next,ItemPickup:GetChildren() do
						local name = v:GetAttribute('itemName')
						if v:GetAttribute('isReady') then
							table.insert(cache, v);
						end
					end
				end
			end
			return cache;
		end)
		function newSound(s,l)
			local v3sound = getLoader('v3sound')
			local v12 = v3sound.newSound(s);
			v12:attachToPart(l)
			v12:play();
		end
		local useCon = v084('require')(ReplicatedStorage.devv.client.Objects.v3item.bin.Consumable.modules.controller.modules.itemFuncs.Present)

		function itemFarmer(TABLECHECK)
			local inventory = getLoader('v3item').inventory
			for _, datav in next,inventory.getItemsData() do
				if (datav and (datav.isStashed ~= true) and table.find(TABLECHECK,datav.name)) then
					local irr = inventory.getFromName(datav.name)
					equip(datav.guid)
					if irr and irr.equipped then
						useCon({item =datav})
					end
				elseif (getgenv().autoCleanInventory == true) then
					local v89444 = selectedMask == datav.name
					local v85798 = selectedVest == datav.name
					local ut4 = utBuy == datav.name
					local ev =datav.name == 'RPG' and rpgBotKill == true or selectedGunBot == datav.name and gunKillBot == true or selectedallplrmodeGun == datav.name and allPlayerOptionToggledGuns == true or selectedallplrsinglemodeGun == datav.name and PlayerActionToggled == true 
					-- if table.find(trashItems33, datav.name) and datav.name ~= selectedFoodfunc and not ev and not ut4 and not v89444 and not v85798 then
					if table.find(trashItems33, datav.name) and datav.name ~= selectedFoodfunc and not removercheck(datav) and not v89444 and not v85798 then

						removeItem(datav.guid);
					end
				end
			end
		end

		getDoor = LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function(kind)
			local dd = workspace:FindFirstChild('Game')
			if dd then
				for l,v in next, workspace.Game.Props.Door:GetChildren() do
					if v:GetAttribute('keycardName') == kind then
						return v,v:GetAttribute('locked')
					end
				end
			end
			return nil,nil
		end)

		function checkItemClaimable(doortype, scanSize, itemclaim)
			local e = workspace:FindFirstChild('Game')
			if e then
				if skipLockedItems ~= true then
					return true 
				end
				local part, islocked = getDoor(doortype)
				if not part or not islocked then
					return true
				end
				local position = part.PrimaryPart and part.PrimaryPart.position
				if not position then
					return true
				end
				local partsInBox = workspace:GetPartBoundsInBox(CFrame.new(position), scanSize)
				local Players = players
				local function isPlayerPart(part)
					local character = part:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
					return character and Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(character) ~= nil
				end
				for _, v in next, partsInBox do
					if not isPlayerPart(v) and v:IsDescendantOf(workspace.Game.Entities.ItemPickup) then
						local attribute = v:GetAttribute('itemName') or (v.Parent and v.Parent:GetAttribute('itemName'))
						if attribute == itemclaim then
							return false
						end
					end
				end
			end
			return true
		end

		CFrameLookAT = function(PrimaryPart,b)
			if not PrimaryPart then return end
			local targetPosition = PrimaryPart.Position
			local desiredCFrame = PrimaryPart.CFrame * b or CFrame.new(0, 0, -10)
			local characterPosition = desiredCFrame.Position
			local distance = (playerHumanoidRootPart.Position - targetPosition).Magnitude
			playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame =CFrame.lookAt(characterPosition, targetPosition)				
		end

			function getSkins()
				local skint = {}
				if getLoader('skins') and getLoader('skins').skinData then
					local skindata = getLoader("skins").skinData
					for l,v in next, skindata  do
						table.insert(skint,l)
					end
					table.sort(skint)
				end
				return skint
			end

			securepcall(function()
				indexUIObj("inventory", "throwairdrops", z001.inventory:Toggle({Title='auto throw airdrops',Value=WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get('autothrowdrops') ,Type="Toggle",Callback=function(state)
					if z001.inventory.throwairdrops ~= nil then
						WindUI.saveDataSettings:LoadDataIf('autothrowdrops',state)
					end					
					getgenv().autoThrowAirdrops = state
					while getgenv().autoThrowAirdrops == true do
						local load = getLoader
						local v3item = load('v3item')
						local oldpos = farmmodes == 'regular' and playerHumanoidRootPart.CFrame or CFrame.new(1653.3216552734375, -16.953155517578125, -529.6856079101562);
						local ce = CFrame.new(1748.92334, 6.21852636, -314.072571, 0.187937602, -8.09037815e-08, 0.982180953, 8.82680027e-08, 1, 6.54817214e-08, -0.982180953, 7.4388673e-08, 0.187937602)
						local inventory = v3item.inventory
						if isnotalreadyfarming() then
							for  l,v in next,{
								'Airdrop Marker',
								'Airstrike Marker',
								'Santa Signal'
							} do
								local hasItem = inventory.getFromName(v)
								if hasItem then
									equip(hasItem.guid)
								-- else
									
								--     InvokeServer('attemptPurchase','Airdrop Marker')

								end
								if hasItem and hasItem.equipped then
									getgenv().isAirdropThrowing = true
									CFrameTP(ce)
									task.wait(1.1)
									for i = 1,3 do
										throwItem({[1]=hasItem.guid,[2]=Vector3.new(0, 0, 0),[3]=Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)})
									end
									task.delay(0.7,function()
										FireServer('removeItem',hasItem.guid)
										inventory.remove(hasItem.guid)   
										getgenv().isAirdropThrowing = false
										CFrameTP(oldpos)
									end)
								end
							end
						end
						task.wait(.5)
					end
				end}));

						"Gold Deagle",
						"Gold AK-47",
						"Diamond Glock",
						"Gravity Gun"
					}

						for l,v in next,inventory and inventory.items or {} do
							if v.type and v.type == "Gun" and not table.find(noskin,v.name) then
								inventory.skinUpdate(v.name,state)
							end
						end
					end
				end}));

			function loccframes()
				if workspace:FindFirstChild('LandmarkNodes') then
					local f = workspace.LandmarkNodes.Nodes
					local nodes={}
					for l,v in next,f:GetChildren() do
						nodes[v.Name] = v.CFrame
					end
					table.sort(nodes)
					return nodes
				else
					return {}
				end
			end
			local tweenstyles = {"Exponential","Sine","Linear","Bounce","Back","Quad","Quart","Quint","Elastic","Circular","Cubic"};
			table.sort(tweenstyles)
			local locnames = {};
			for k, x in pairs(loccframes()) do
				table.insert(locnames, k);
				table.sort(locnames);
			end
			local randcframe = {};
			for z, s in next, loccframes() do
				table.insert(randcframe, s);
			end
			function tweenstylefunc()
				if (tweenstyless ~= nil) then
					return Enum.EasingStyle[tweenstyless];
				else
					return Enum.EasingStyle.Linear;
				end
			end

			function setCharacterVelocityToZero()
				for _, part in ipairs(playerCharacter:GetDescendants()) do
					if part:IsA("BasePart") then
						part.Velocity =  Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
					end
				end
			end

			function GetTradeCountdown(player)
				local v19 = getLoader('globals')
				local minAgeDays = v19.TRADING and v19.TRADING.MIN_ACCOUNT_AGE or 0
				local accountAge = player.AccountAge or 0
				local remainingDays = minAgeDays - accountAge
				if v19.TRADING then
					if remainingDays <= 0 then
						return "You can trade now!"
					else
						local totalHours = remainingDays * 24
						local days = math.floor(totalHours / 24)
						local hours = math.floor(totalHours % 24)
						local minutes = math.floor((totalHours * 60) % 60)
						return string.format("%d days", days)
					end
				else
					return ''
				end
			end
			if GetTradeCountdown(lp) ~= 'You can trade now!' then
				getgenv().cantTrade = true
				indexUIObj("playerinfo", "skinLog", z001.playerinfo:Paragraph({Title="player logs",Desc=getSkinLogString(cantTrade,GetTradeCountdown(lp))}));
			else
				indexUIObj("playerinfo", "skinLog", z001.playerinfo:Paragraph({Title="player logs",Desc=getSkinLogString()}));
			end
			indexUIObj("playerinfo", "inventoryLog", z001.playerinfo:Paragraph({Title="inventory logs",Desc=getInventoryLog()}));

				local connection = loadU:GetConnection('PlayerInformationUpdate')
				if not connection then
					loadU:CreateConnection("PlayerInformationUpdate", RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(LPH_NO_VIRTUALIZE(function()
						local result, _ = pcall(function()
							local currentTime = tick();
							if ((currentTime - lastOverallUpdateTime) >= overallUpdateInterval) then
								lastOverallUpdateTime = currentTime;
								refreshAllPlayerData();
								if (z001.playerinfo and z001.playerinfo.skinLog and z001.playerinfo.skinLog.SetDesc) then
									z001.playerinfo.skinLog:SetDesc(getSkinLogString(cantTrade,(function()

											return nil
										end
									end)()));
								end
								if (z001.playerinfo.inventoryLog and (z001.playerinfo.inventoryLog.SetDesc ~= nil)) then
									z001.playerinfo.inventoryLog:SetDesc(getInventoryLog());
								end
								if (z001.playerinfo.banBool and z001.playerinfo.banBool.SetDesc) then
									if (isBanActive == true) then
										if (isBanActive or (banEND_unix and (banEND_unix > (currentTime - 10)))) then
											z001.playerinfo.banBool:SetDesc(getString("realbanlog"));
										elseif not isBanActive then
											z001.playerinfo.banBool:SetDesc("shadowbanActive: false\nban-count: " .. numshadowbans .. "\nbannedfrom: " .. getlastban(shadowbanned_by, numshadowbans, shadowbanned_reason) .. "\ntimeLeft: ban has expired or is not active.");
										end
									end
								end
							end
						end);
						if (result == false) then
							v084('warn')(result,_)
							loadU:CleanConnectionIf("PlayerInformationUpdate", result);
							result = nil;
						end
					end)));
				end
			end}));

		local d = getLoader('mobileDealer')
		local mathrand = math.random(5000,7000)
		local itemsToAdd = {
			Gun = {'Acid Gun','Snowball Launcher'},
			Misc = {'Saber'},
			Throwable = {'C5', 'Heavy C4'}
		}
		for category, items in pairs(itemsToAdd) do
			for _, item in pairs(d[category]) do
				item.stock = mathrand
			end
			for _, itemName in pairs(items) do
				local exists = false
				for _, item in pairs(d[category]) do
					if item.itemName == itemName then
						exists = true
						break
					end
				end
				if not exists then
					table.insert(d[category], {stock = mathrand, itemName = itemName})
				end
			end
		end
		function unlockEmotes(v43)
			local v4 = getLoader
			local v10 = v4('emotes')
			local v16 = {
				"free", 
				"premiumEmotes"
			};
			local v9 = v4("GUILoader");
			local v18;
			repeat 
				task.wait() 
				v18 = v9.Get("Emotes") 
			until v18:FindFirstChild('Frame') and v18.Frame:FindFirstChild('ScrollingFrame') or v18:WaitForChild('Frame') and v18.Frame:WaitForChild('ScrollingFrame') or v9 and v9.Get ~= nil and v9.Get('Emotes') and v9.Get('Emotes'):FindFirstChild('Frame')
			for v44, v45 in pairs(v10) do
				if v16[v45.category or 1] == v43 then
					local v46
					repeat
						task.wait()
						v46 = v18.Frame.ScrollingFrame:FindFirstChild(v44)
					until v46
					v46.Holder.Locked.Visible = false;
					if loadU:GetConnection(tostring(v44)) == false then
						loadU:CreateConnection(tostring(v44),v46.Holder.Locked:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Visible"):Connect(function()
							if v46.Holder.Locked.Visible then
								v46.Holder.Locked.Visible = false;
								return
							end
						end));
					end
				end
			end
		end
		task.spawn(unlockEmotes,'premiumEmotes')
		local v0 = WindUI.saveDataSettings.Get('uiScale',true) or 0.8
		getgenv().uiScaler = tonumber(v0)		
		task.delay(1.5,function()
			WindUI:SetUIScale(uiScaler)

		end)
		ShowChatLogs(true);
		local r , P = pcall(function()
			local data = getLoader('state').data
			-- for l,v in next,data do v084('warn')(l,v) end
			if data and data.testAPIBan then
				local banAPI = data.testAPIBan					
				local reason = banAPI.reason
				local banTime =banAPI.banTime
				local duration =banAPI.duration		
				local s = ("```" .. "reason: " .. reason .. "\nbanTime: " .. banTime .. "\nduration: " .. duration .. "```")								
				v084('warn')('DETECTED: @'..getLoader('state').data.testAPIBan.reason)
				return s
			elseif data and not data.testAPIBan then
				return ('```' .. 'currently undetected!' .. '```')
			end
		end)
		if not r then 
			v084('warn')(P)
			P = ''
		end				
		local result, _ = pcall(__loadNow.sendInjectionSuccessful, TeTraXSessionID,P);
		if result then
			v084('warn')("Welcome...");

		else
			v084('warn')(result,_)
		end
	end
else
	__loadNow.sendErrorLog("EXECUTOR NOT SUPPORTED",'9013');
